 
aɟa്ɲaːt̪anṯe bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪ajuʈe pa്ɾaോɟaka്ṯṯa് ɡuʈa്ʈanbarɡa് ibuka്ka്

iː ibuka്ka് aːrka്kum eʋiʈejum t͡ʃelaʋila്laːt̪e upajaോɡika്kaːnuɭa്ɭat̪aːɳa്
mika്kaʋaːrum n̪ijana്t̪a്ɾaɳaŋa്ŋaɭaൊn̪a്n̪umila്la n̪iŋa്ŋaɭka്ka് it̪a് pakart̪a്t̪ukajaോ n̪alkukajaോ t͡ʃeja്jaːm
pa്ɾaോɟaka്ṯṯa് ɡuʈa്ʈanbarɡa് lai̯sansa് uɭpa്peʈut̪a്t̪ijiʈa്ʈuɭa്ɭa n̪ibana്ɖʱanakaɭka്ka് kiːɻil it̪a് ʋiːɳa്ʈum upajaോɡika്kuka
iː ibuka്kinaൊpa്pam ala്leŋa്kil l oːɳlai̯naːji


t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈa് bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪a

ɾat͡ʃajit̪aːʋa് aɟa്ɲaːt̪an

ʋiʋart̪a്t̪akan sar eɖa്ʋin arn̪aോɭɖa്

paോsa്ṯṯa് t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪a t̪iːjat̪i ɟuːɳ    #
riliːsa് t̪iːjat̪i n̪aʋambar 
aːd̪a്jam paോsa്ṯṯa് t͡ʃeja്t̪at̪a് ɟanuʋaɾi

pa്ɾat̪iːka seṯṯa് enkaോɖimɡa്

krɨʂa്ɳanum arɟun ɾaːɟakumaːɾanum oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪ar pa്ɾabʱaːʂaɳam n̪aʈat̪a്t̪i

aːmukʰam
iː pa്ɾasid̪a്ɖʱaʋum at̪iʃajakaɾaʋumaːja samsa്krɨt̪a kaːʋa്jam maɦaːbʱaːɾat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe oɾu epa്pisaോɖaːji sambʱaʋika്kuna്n̪u aːraːmat̪a്t̪e  ala്leŋa്kil bʱiːʂa്ma  maɦat̪a്t̪aːja ɦina്d̪uː it̪iɦaːsat̪a്t̪inṯe parʋa്ʋat̪a്t̪il d̪eːʋanaːɡiɾi saːɦit̪a്jat̪a്t̪ile paɲa്t͡ʃaɾat̪a്‌n̪anipaɲa്t͡ʃaɾat̪a്‌n̪aŋa്ŋaɭil ona്n̪aːji kaɳaka്kaːka്kapa്peʈuna്n̪a ina്t̪a്jajil at̪a് ʋalija ɟanapa്ɾiːt̪ijum aɖʱikaːɾaʋum aːsa്ʋad̪ika്kuna്n̪u ʋa്jaka്t̪aʋum ena്n̪aːl ʃa്ɾeːʂa്ʈʰaʋumaːja bʱaːʂajil at̪a് ina്n̪um n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪a ba്ɾaːɦa്maɳamaːji n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪a oɾu d̪aːrʃanika ʋa്jaʋasa്t̪ʰaje ʋikasipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeʈuka്kuna്n̪u ʋiʃa്ʋaːsam kapila pat̪aɲa്ɟali ʋeːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭ ena്n̪iʋajuʈe sid̪a്ɖʱaːna്t̪aŋa്ŋaɭe paോle samana്ʋajipa്pika്kuna്n̪u at̪inṯe pa്ɾakʰa്jaːpanaŋa്ŋaɭil palat̪um ʋaɭaɾe ujarn̪a്n̪at̪aːɳa് at̪inṯe abʱilaːʂaŋa്ŋaɭ ʋaɭaɾe ʃud̪a്ɖʱaʋum aːrd̪a്ɾaʋumaːɳa് ʂa്leɡal t̪anṯe kaʋit̪ajeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuɭa്ɭa paʈʰanat̪a്t̪ina് ʃeːʂam at̪ileːka്ka് kaʈaka്kuna്n̪u at̪inṯe aɟa്ɲaːt̪a ɾat͡ʃajit̪aːʋinaോʈuɭa്ɭa aːɦa്laːd̪at̪a്t̪inṯejum pa്ɾaʃamsajuʈejum iː paൊʈa്ʈit̪a്t̪eri maɟisa്‌ʈa്ɾaോram reʋarenʂa്ja e ba്ɾaːt͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്‌maɳisa് inṯar saːnsisa്sima pijaːṯṯisa് oːfiːsa് rafart̪ur erɡaോ ʈe pa്ɾai̯mam ʋaːṯṯa്sa് saːnsisai̯m n̪a്juːminisa്ka് ɦai̯pa്paോfeṯṯa                    kam         iː maɦat̪a്t̪aːja aːd̪aɾaːɲa്ɟali pa്ɾat̪iɖʱa്ʋanika്kuna്n̪u t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum ʋaɭaɾe ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱeːjamaːɳa് iʋiʈejuɭa്ɭa t͡ʃila ɖʱaːrma്mikat̪akaɭ ʋaɭaɾe ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱeːjamaːɳa് at̪inaːl samaːna്t̪aɾat̪aje aʈaja്ka്kuna്n̪u  palapa്paോɻum ʋaːka്kaːluɭa്ɭa  at̪inṯe paʈʰipa്pika്kalukaɭka്kum put̪ija n̪ijamat̪a്t̪inum iʈajil paɳa്ɖiṯṯukaɭum miʂaɳarimaːɾum t̪ama്mil oɾu t̪arka്kam ujarn̪a്n̪u ɾat͡ʃajit̪aːʋa് ka്ɾisa്t̪a്jan sa്ɾaോt̪asa്sukaɭil n̪ina്n̪aːɳaോ at̪aോ suʋiʃeːʂakaɾum apa്paോsa്t̪alana്maːɾum aʋanil n̪ina്n̪a് kaʈameʈut̪a്t̪at̪aːɳaോ ena്n̪a ʋiʂajat̪a്t̪il

it̪a് at̪inṯe t̪iːjat̪ijeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuɭa്ɭa t͡ʃaോd̪a്jam ujart̪a്t̪una്n̪u at̪a് ka്ɾijaːt̪a്makamaːji paɾiɦaɾika്kaːn kaɻijila്la jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa maɦaːbʱaːɾat̪at̪a്t̪eːka്kaːɭ pina്n̪iːʈuɭa്ɭa kaːlaɡʱaʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪il it̪a് puɾaːt̪ana it̪iɦaːsat̪a്t̪il uɭpa്peʈut̪a്t̪ijiɾika്kaɳam ena്n̪aːl ka്ɾisa്t̪a്jan kaːlaɡʱaʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪ina് muma്puɭa്ɭat̪aːɳena്n̪a് t̪eɭijika്kaːn kaːʃinaːt̪ʰa് t̪elaːmɡa് t͡ʃila n̪a്jaːjamaːja ʋaːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭ aʋat̪aɾipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ena്n̪iɾuna്n̪aːlum t̪eɭiʋukaɭuʈe bʱaːɾam ka്ɾisa്t̪uʋina് ʃeːʂamuɭa്ɭa muːna്n̪aːm n̪uːṯṯaːɳa്ʈilaːɳa് at̪inṯe ɡʱaʈana sa്t̪ʰaːpika്kuna്n̪at̪a് oɾupaka്ʂeː iː ba്ɾaːɦa്maɳa kaːʋa്jat̪a്t̪il ɡaliːlijuʈe paːʈʰaŋa്ŋaɭuʈejum sirijan aʋat̪aːɾat̪a്t̪inṯejum pa്ɾat̪iɖʱa്ʋanikaɭ ʃaɾika്kum uɳa്ʈaːjeːka്kaːm

ɟuma്‌n̪aja്ka്kum sarsuːʈa്ʈi n̪ad̪ikaɭka്kum iʈajiluɭa്ɭa n̪iɾapa്paːja ɾaːɟa്jamaːɳa് at̪inṯe d̪rɨʃa്jamipa്paോɭ kurn̪uːlinum ɟiːna്d̪inum juɖʱiʂa്ʈʰiɾa ɾaːɟaːʋinṯe saɦaോd̪aɾan arɟa്ɟunan ɾaːɟakumaːɾan saːɾat̪ʰijuʈe ʋeːʂam ɖʱaɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa paɾamaോn̪a്n̪at̪a d̪eːʋanaːja krɨʂa്ɳanumaːji n̪aʈat̪a്t̪ija sambʱaːʂaɳamaːɳa് it̪inṯe laɭit̪amaːja it̪iʋrɨt̪a്t̪am kau̯ɾaʋaɾuʈejum paːɳa്ɖaʋaɾuʈejum sai̯na്jaŋa്ŋaɭ t̪ama്mil oɾu ʋalija jud̪a്ɖʱam aːsana്n̪amaːjiɾika്kuna്n̪u et̪ir sai̯na്jaŋa്ŋaɭ t̪ama്miluɭa്ɭa jud̪a്ɖʱaɾat̪ʰat̪a്t̪ilaːɳa് iː sambʱaːʂaɳam n̪aʈaka്kuna്n̪at̪a്

kaʋit̪aje barn̪uːfa് fa്ɾaɲa്t͡ʃileːka്kum laːsan laːṯṯinileːka്kum iṯṯaːlijan sa്ṯṯaːnisa്laːʋa് ɡaːʈa്ʈijileːka്kum ɡalanaോsa് ɡa്ɾiːka്kileːka്kum misa്ṯṯar t̪aോmsaɳum misa്ṯṯar ɖeːʋisum imɡa്liːʂileːka്kum aʋasaːnamaːji peːɾiʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪at̪inṯe ɡad̪a്ja ʈa്ɾaːnsa്ka്ɾipa്ṯṯileːka്kum maːṯṯijiɾika്kuna്n̪u at̪inṯe ʋiʃa്ʋasa്t̪at̪ajum ʋa്jaka്t̪at̪ajum misa്ṯṯar t̪elaːmɡa് baോmbejil oɾu sambʱaːʂaɳa t̪aːɭat̪a്t̪il oɾu pat̪ipa്pa് pa്ɾasid̪a്ɖʱiːkaɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu at̪a് n̪ana്n̪aːji paʈʰit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪um bud̪a്ɖʱipaɾaʋumaːɳa് ena്n̪aːl oriɟinalinṯe maːna്jat̪ajaോ krɨpajaോ arijika്kuna്n̪ila്la n̪iɾaʋaɖʱi una്n̪at̪a paɳa്ɖit̪ana്maːrka്ka് ʃeːʂam at̪iʃajakaɾamaːja kaʋit̪ajuʈe ʋiʋart̪a്t̪anam n̪alkaːn ɲaːn t̪uniɲa്ɲaːl at̪a് aʋaɾuʈe aɖʱa്ʋaːnat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് uɾut̪a്t̪iɾiɲa്ɲa saɦaːjat̪a്t̪inuɭa്ɭa krɨt̪aɟa്ɲat̪aːpaɾamaːja amɡiːkaːɾamaːɳa് maːt̪a്ɾamala്la ɟanapa്ɾijamaːja oɾu kaːʋa്jaːt̪a്makaʋum d̪aːrʃanikaʋumaːja oɾu krɨt̪i ila്leŋa്kil imɡa്liːʂa് saːɦit̪a്jam t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum apuːrɳa്ɳamaːjiɾika്kum ina്t̪a്jajileːka്ka്

saോmɡa് selasa്ṯṯijal sa്ʋajam ʋiʃad̪iːkaɾika്kaːt̪a്t̪a maṯṯaൊn̪a്n̪um parajaːnila്la paːʃa്t͡ʃaːt̪a്ja t͡ʃeʋikaɭka്kaːji ʋiɟajakaɾamaːji punarn̪irma്mika്kaːn kaɻijaːt̪a്t̪a anuʂa്ʈubʱa് miːṯṯarilaːɳa് samsa്krɨt̪a muːlakrɨt̪i eɻut̪ijiɾika്kuna്n̪at̪a് at̪inaːl ɲaːn at̪ine ɲaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ʋaɻaka്kamuɭa്ɭa ʃuːna്jamaːja ʋaːka്jat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് iʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪u ʋaːt͡ʃakam t̪ana്n̪e at̪eːpaോle t̪akaɾuna്n̪a ɡaːnaɾat͡ʃanaː aɭaʋukaɭaːji maːruna്n̪u mika്kaʋaːrum inipa്parajuna്n̪a peːɟukaɭil ina്d̪a്ɾijam ʋiʃa്ʋasa്t̪at̪ajaോʈe samɾaka്ʂika്kapa്peʈumena്n̪a് ɲaːn ʋiʃa്ʋasika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪aːl ʂa്leɡal t̪ana്n̪e iŋa്ŋane parajeːɳa്ʈi ʋana്n̪u in riːkaɳa്ʈiːjaോribasa് mi sema്par paൊjaṯṯaːfaോsa്ṯṯar menṯam reka്ʈeː ɖiʋinaːsa്se afirmajar n̪aോɳ oːsim kaʋit̪ajuʈe t̪at̪a്t̪a്ʋat͡ʃina്t̪ajeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് kuːʈut̪al ʋaːjika്kaːn aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kuna്n̪aʋarka്ka് mesa്seːɻa്sa് ʈa്ɾaba്n̪ar & kaോ at͡ʃa്t͡ʃaʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa misa്ṯṯar ɖeːʋiːsinṯe ʋaːla്jat̪a്t̪il pa്ɾaʃamsaniːjamaːja oɾu aːmukʰam kaɳa്ʈet̪a്t̪aːm

saɲa്ɟaja

pina്n̪e iː ʋaːka്kukaɭ paraɲa്ɲu oː ɡuɾuʋeː iː ʋaɾi kaːɳuka

d̪a്ɾupad̪an t̪anṯe kaːril pa്ɾamukʰan
ɖʱrɨʂa്ʈakeːt̪a് t͡ʃeːkit̪an kaːʃijuʈe t̪aʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa pa്ɾabʱu
puɾuɟit̪a്t̪a് kuna്t̪ibʱaോɟa് ʃai̯ʋa്ja
juɖʱaːmana്juʋinaൊpa്pam ut̪a്t̪amau̯ɟa്
subʱad̪a്ɾajuʈe kuʈa്ʈi opa്pam d̪a്ɾupat̪ijuʈeela്laːm pa്ɾaʃasa്t̪i
ela്laːʋaɾum aʋaɾuʈe t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪a ɾat̪ʰaŋa്ŋaɭil kajaruna്n̪u
ɲaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe bʱaːɡat̪a്t̪um n̪iː ba്ɾaːɦa്maɳaɾil ut̪a്t̪aman kaːɳuka
mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa meːɖʱaːʋikaɭ enṯe lai̯nile kamaːnɖarmaːr
aːɾuʈe peːɾukaɭ eɳa്ɳuna്n̪at̪il ɲaːn sana്t̪aോʂika്kuna്n̪u n̪iː t̪ana്n̪e aːd̪a്jat̪a്t̪eːt̪a്
apa്paോɭ bʱiːʂa്mar karɳa്ɳan krɨpan jud̪a്ɖʱat̪a്t̪il uɡa്ɾan
ʋikarɳa്ɳan aʃa്ʋat̪a്t̪ʰaːman iʋajuʈe aʈut̪a്t̪a്
kaɾut̪a്t̪uṯṯa sau̯mad̪at̪a്t̪i n̪iraje ʋeːrejum
ɖʱiːɾanum ʃa്ɾamit͡ʃa്t͡ʃum maɾika്kaːn iː d̪iʋasam t̪aja്jaːraːɳa്
enika്kaːji aʋaɾuʈe ɾaːɟaːʋa് oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪an aːjuɖʱam piʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
oːɾaോ meːkʰalajilum kaɻiʋuɭa്ɭaʋar eːṯṯaʋum d̪urbalamaːjat̪a്
bʱiːʂa്mar eʋiʈejaːɳa് aːɟa്ɲaːpika്kuna്n̪at̪ena്n̪a് n̪ama്muʈe jud̪a്ɖʱam kaːɳika്kuna്n̪u
bʱiːman aʋanṯe muna്n̪il ʋaɭaɾe ʃaka്t̪amaːja ona്n̪a്
bʱiːʂa്maɾuʈe n̪iɾajaോʈa് aʈut̪a്t̪iɾika്kuna്n̪a n̪ama്muʈe n̪aːjakana്maːɾe paɾipaːlika്kuka
aʋarka്ka് ena്t̪a് saɦaːjamaːɳa് t͡ʃeja്jaːn kaɻijuka ena്n̪a് t̪aja്jaːraːka്kuka ipa്paോɭ enṯe ʂel uːt̪uka
apa്paോɭ ʋrɨd̪a്ɖʱanaːja ɾaːɟaːʋinṯe suːt͡ʃanajil
ɾaka്t̪am uɳart̪a്t̪aːn aːka്ɾaോʃat̪a്t̪aോʈe t͡ʃuṯṯum uɾuɭuna്n̪u
kaːɦaɭaka്kaːɾanaːja simɦaɡarɟa്ɟanam paോle
ʋalija ʃamkʰa് uːt̪i opa്pam at̪inṯe baɦaɭat̪a്t̪il
kaːɦaɭam t̪aːɭam kai̯t̪a്t̪aːɭam ɡaോŋa്ŋa് kaൊma്pukaɭ
peʈa്ʈena്n̪uɭa്ɭa baɦaɭat̪a്t̪il paൊʈa്ʈit̪a്t̪erit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu sa്faോʈanaŋa്ŋaɭ paോle
ajaɲa്ɲa kaൊʈuŋa്kaːṯṯil at̪a്t̪aɾamaൊɾu kaോlaːɦalam t̪aോn̪a്n̪i
apa്paോɭ aʋaɾuʈe sa്ʋarɳa്ɳa kaːril kaɳa്ʈeːka്kaːm
ʋeɭut̪a്t̪a kut̪iɾakaɭaːl n̪ukat̪a്t̪il aʋaɾuʈe jud̪a്ɖʱa ʂela്lukaɭ uːt̪i
krɨʂa്ɳan d̪ai̯ʋam arɟa്ɟunan aʋanṯe aɾikil
krɨʂa്ɳan keʈa്ʈaɻit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa puːʈa്ʈukaɭaോʈe t̪anṯe ʋalija ʃamkʰa് uːt̪i
bʱiːmanṯe asa്t̪ʰi kaൊt̪a്t̪ijeʈut̪a്t̪at̪a് arɟunan uːt̪i
ina്d̪a്ɾanṯe ut͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്t̪iluɭa്ɭa sama്maːnam bʱiːman bʱajaŋa്kaɾan
t͡ʃena്n̪aːjaʋajaṯṯuɭa്ɭa bʱiːmanoɾu n̪iːɳa്ʈa iːra ʃamkʰa് uːt̪i
kuna്t̪ijuʈe kuṯṯamaṯṯa put̪a്ɾanaːja juɖʱiʂa്ʈʰiɾanum
oɾu ʃaka്t̪amaːja ʂel kaːṯṯaʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ʋiɟajat̪a്t̪inṯe ʃaba്d̪am
n̪akulan t̪anṯe ʃamkʰil ɾaോd̪anam muɻaka്ki
maɖʱuɾamaːja ʃaba്d̪am ena്n̪a് peːɾiʈa്ʈat̪a് saɦad̪eːʋa് t̪anṯe meːl
ɾat̪a്n̪aŋa്ŋaɭaːl alaŋa്kaɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa ena്n̪a് ʋiɭika്kapa്peʈuna്n̪u kaːʃijuʈe ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
ʃikʰaɳa്ɖi t̪anṯe kaːril ɖʱrɨʂa്ʈad̪a്juma്n̪an
ʋiɾaːʈan kiːɻaʈaŋa്ŋaːt̪a്t̪a saːt̪a്jaki
d̪a്ɾupad̪an t̪anṯe put̪a്ɾana്maːɾaോʈaൊpa്pam bʱuːmijuʈe n̪aːt̪ʰaː
n̪iːɳa്ʈa kai̯kaɭuɭa്ɭa subʱad̪a്ɾajuʈe maka്kaɭ ela്laːʋaɾum ut͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്t̪il uːt̪i
aŋa്ŋane ka്laːŋa്kaോr aʋaɾuʈe ʃat̪a്ɾuka്kaɭuʈe ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪e kuluka്ki
kuluŋa്ŋuna്n̪a bʱuːmijaോʈum iʈimuɻaka്kat̪a്t̪aോʈum kuːʈi
apa്paോɭ at̪a്
ɖʱrɨt̪iɾaːʂa്‌ʈa്ɾanṯe jud̪a്ɖʱasaɲa്t͡ʃajam kaɳa്ʈa്
aːjuɖʱaŋa്ŋaɭ aɻit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeʈuka്kuna്n̪u ʋila്lukaɭ ujart̪a്t̪i jud̪a്ɖʱam
t̪alka്ʂaɳam t̪akarka്kaːnarɟun at̪inṯe ensai̯nbaːɖa്ɟa്
ɦanumaːn kuɾaŋa്ŋanaːɳaോ it̪a് paraɲa്ɲat̪a്
t̪anṯe saːɾat̪ʰijaːja d̪iʋa്janaːja krɨʂa്ɳanaോʈa്
ɖʱai̯ɾa്jamila്laːt̪a്t̪aʋaneː t̪urasa്saːja sa്t̪ʰalat̪a്t̪eːka്ka് oːʈika്kuka
sai̯na്jaŋa്ŋaɭka്kiʈajil ɲaːn kuːʈut̪al aʈut̪a്t̪a് kaːɳum
n̪ama്maോʈa് jud̪a്ɖʱam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪aʋaɾe n̪ama്maɭ kaൊla്laɳam
ina്n̪a് jud̪a്ɖʱat̪a്t̪inṯe maɖʱa്jasa്t̪ʰat̪ajil t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum
iː samat̪alat̪a്t̪il t̪iŋa്ŋika്kuːʈuna്n̪a ela്laːʋaɾum ɾaka്t̪at͡ʃa്t͡ʃaൊɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃilil kuniɲa്ɲiɾika്kuna്n̪u
ɖʱrɨt̪iɾaːʂa്ʈa്ɾaɾuʈe paːpijaːja put̪a്ɾane anusaɾika്kuna്n̪u
aŋa്ŋane arɟa്ɟunan pa്ɾaːrt̪a്t̪ʰit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ɦeː bʱaɾat̪a
aː sa്ʋarɡa്ɡiːja saːɾat̪ʰi sai̯na്jaŋa്ŋaɭka്kiʈajil
t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪a kaːr oːʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu at̪inṯe paːlʋeɭut̪a്t̪a sa്ṯṯiːɖukaɭe t̪aʈaɲa്ɲunirt̪a്t̪i
bʱiːʂa്maɾum d̪a്ɾaോɳaɾum aʋaɾuʈe n̪aːt̪ʰana്maːɾum n̪ajit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്
kaːɳuka aʋan arɟa്ɟunan̪aോʈa് paraɲa്ɲu aʋar eʋiʈe n̪ilka്kuna്n̪u
aŋa്ŋajuʈe kuɾuna്n̪ukaɭ ɾaːɟakumaːɾanum
oːɾaോ kai̯jilum aʋanṯe ʋiːʈa്ʈile bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭe aʈajaːɭapa്peʈut̪a്t̪i
mut̪a്t̪aʃa്ʃimaːɾum at͡ʃa്t͡ʃana്maːɾum ama്maːʋana്maːɾum saɦaോd̪aɾana്maːɾum maka്kaɭum
kasinsum maɾumaka്kaɭum maɾumaka്kaɭum miʃa്ɾaɳam
suɦrɨt̪a്t̪uka്kaɭaോʈum baɦumaːnapa്peʈa്ʈa mut̪irn̪a്n̪aʋaɾaോʈum opa്pam t͡ʃilar iː ʋaʃat̪a്t̪a്
t͡ʃilar aː ʋaʃam paɾana്n̪u et̪irka്kuna്n̪aʋaɾe kaɳa്ʈiʈa്ʈa്
at̪a്t̪aɾam kit̪a്t̪a് ʋaɭarn̪a്n̪uʋana്n̪a ʃat̪a്ɾuka്kaɭarɟunanṯe ɦrɨd̪ajam
saɦat̪aːpam kaൊɳa്ʈa് uɾuki aʋan iŋa്ŋane paraɲa്ɲu
arɟa്ɟunan
krɨʂa്ɳaː ɲaːn kaːɳuna്n̪at̪upaോle iʋiʈe t͡ʃaൊɾijaːn ʋaɾuː
aʋaɾuʈe paൊt̪u ɾaka്t̪am n̪ama്muʈe bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭuʈe kuːʈa്ʈaːja്ma
enṯe aʋajaʋaŋa്ŋaɭ paɾaːɟajapa്peʈuna്n̪u enṯe n̪aːʋa് enṯe ʋaːjil ʋaɾaɳa്ʈupaോkuna്n̪u
oɾu ʋirajal enṯe ʃaɾiːɾat̪a്t̪ejum muʈijejum puɭakam kaൊɭa്ɭika്kuna്n̪u
bʱajaːnakamaːja kuṯṯiɾaോmaŋa്ŋaɭ enṯe d̪urbalamaːja kai̯ ʋaɻuʋukaɭil n̪ina്n̪a്
ɡaːɳa്ɖiːʋa് n̪ala്la ʋila്lu oɾu pani kat̪a്t̪una്n̪u
enṯe t̪a്ʋaka്ka് ʋaɾaɳa്ʈupaോkuna്n̪u enika്ka് n̪ilka്kaːn pa്ɾajaːsamaːɳa്
enṯe uɭa്ɭile ɟiːʋan n̪iːna്t̪i t̪aɭarn̪a്n̪upaോkuna്n̪at̪aːji t̪aോn̪a്n̪una്n̪u
kaʂa്ʈaʋum ʋilaːpaʋum oɻiʋaːka്ki ɲaːn ona്n̪um munkuːʈa്ʈi kaːɳuna്n̪ila്la
at̪a് n̪ala്lat̪ala്la ɦeː keːʃaʋaː n̪ala്lat̪ala്la
paɾasa്paɾamuɭa്ɭa kaʃaːpa്pil n̪ina്n̪a് ut̪a്bʱaʋika്kaːm aja്jaോ ɲaːn ʋeruka്kuna്n̪u
ʋiɟajaʋum aːɖʱipat̪a്jaʋum sama്pat̪a്t̪um eɭupa്paʋum
aŋa്ŋane saŋa്kaʈat̪a്t̪aോʈe ʋiɟajit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu aɦaോ ena്t̪a് ʋiɟajam
aːnan̪a്d̪am n̪alkaːm ɡaോʋina്d̪a ena്t̪a് sama്pana്n̪amaːjat̪a് kaൊɭa്ɭajaʈika്kuna്n̪u
laːbʱamuɳa്ʈaːka്kaːm ena്t̪a് n̪ijamamaːɳa് pa്ɾat̪ipʰalam et̪a്ɾa sa്paːn
ɟiːʋit̪am t̪ana്n̪e maɖʱuɾamaːji t̪aോn̪a്n̪una്n̪u at̪a്t̪aɾam ɾaka്t̪am kaൊɳa്ʈa് ʋaːŋa്ŋijat̪a്
maɾika്kaːn t̪aja്jaːraːji iʋa iʋiʈe n̪ilka്kuna്n̪at̪a് kaɳa്ʈapa്paോɭ
aːɾuʈe n̪imit̪a്t̪am ɟiːʋit̪am n̪a്jaːjaʋum sana്t̪aോʂaʋum aːjiɾuna്n̪u
aɖʱikaːɾam amuːla്jamaːji ʋaɭarn̪a്n̪ukaൊt͡ʃa്t͡ʃumaka്kaɭum pa്ɾabʱuka്kana്maːɾum put̪a്ɾana്maːɾum
saɦaോd̪aɾana്maːɾum ama്maːjijapa്pana്maːɾum maɾumaka്kaɭum

aʋar ɲaŋa്ŋaɭe kaൊla്laːn n̪aോka്kuna്n̪uɳa്ʈeŋa്kilum oɾu aʈijala്la
ɦeː maɖʱusuːd̪anan ɲaːn samaɾam t͡ʃeja്jumaോ

kuṯṯaʋaːɭikaɭ aʋaɾuʈe maɾaɳat̪a്t̪aːl n̪aːm kuṯṯaka്kaːɾaːji ʋaɭaɾum

aː ɖʱrɨt̪iɾaːʂa്ʈa്ɾa put̪a്ɾana്maːɾum ɲaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭum
ɦeː maːɖʱaʋaː at̪ina് ena്t̪a് samaːɖʱaːnamaːɳa് labʱika്kuka
kaːɾaɳam kaːmat̪a്t̪aːlum ka്ɾaോɖʱat̪a്t̪aːlum ana്ɖʱaɾaːjaːl
aʋarka്ka് paːpam kaːɳaːn kaɻijila്la ala്leŋa്kil kaːɳaːn kaɻijila്la
ɾaːɟaʋamʃat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് purat̪a്t̪aːka്kapa്peʈa്ʈaʋaɾum kaൊla്lapa്peʈa്ʈa bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭum
it̪a്t̪aɾamaൊɾu kuṯṯakrɨt̪a്jam kaːɳuna്n̪a n̪ama്maɭ eŋa്ŋane oɻiʋaːka്kaɾut̪a്

manuʂa്jaɾuʈe aːnan̪a്d̪ameː ɟanaːrd̪anaː

aː bʱaʋanat̪a്t̪il aɖʱarma്mam pa്ɾaʋeːʃika്kuna്n̪u

bʱa്ɾaːna്t̪amaːja ʋikaːɾaŋa്ŋaɭ ɟaːt̪ikaɭuʈe kuːʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːɾal
aː kuʈumbat̪a്t̪ina് oɾu n̪aɾaka ʋaɻi ajat͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
d̪uʂa്ʈa ka്ɾaോɖʱat̪a്t̪aːl at̪inṯe n̪aːʃam ʋaɾut̪a്t̪ijaʋan
ala്la baɦumaːnapa്peʈa്ʈa puːrʋa്ʋikaɾuʈe aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭ
aʋaɾuʈe samaːɖʱaːnasa്t̪ʰalat̪a്t̪a് n̪ina്n̪a് ʋiːɳupaോkuka
ʃaʋasamsa്kaːɾa keːka്kukaɭuʈejum ʋaːn ɖet̪a്t̪a്ʋaːʈa്ʈarinṯejum#
at̪inaːl ɲaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱa sa്t̪ut̪ikaɭ paʈʰipa്pika്kuka aŋa്ŋane ɲaŋa്ŋaɭ kaൊla്lukajaːɳeŋa്kil
bʱau̯mika ʃaka്t̪ijuʈe sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inaːji bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭum suɦrɨt̪a്t̪uka്kaɭum
aɦaോʋat̪a് ena്t̪aൊɾu maോʃam t̪eṯṯaːjiɾuna്n̪u at̪a്
enṯe bana്ɖʱuka്kaɭ samaɾam t͡ʃeja്t̪aːl ɲaːn at̪a് kaɾut̪una്n̪u
aːjuɖʱamila്laːt̪e aʋaɾe n̪eːɾiʈaːn enṯe mulakaɭ n̪aɡa്n̪amaːka്kaːn
t̪aɳa്ʈum kuna്t̪aʋum aʈikaൊɳa്ʈa് ut̪a്t̪aɾam n̪alkuna്n̪at̪ineːka്kaːɭ
aŋa്ŋane parajuma്paോɭ aː ɾaɳa്ʈa് aːt̪it̪ʰeːjaɾuʈe mukʰat̪a്t̪a്
arɟa്ɟunan t̪anṯe ɾat̪ʰaːsanat̪a്t̪il muŋa്ŋi
ʋila്lum ama്pum ʋiːɻaʈa്ʈe ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪il asukʰam
iʋiʈe bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪ajuʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam 
arɟunʋiʂaːd̪a് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil arɟunanṯe d̪uɾit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam 
saɲa്ɟaja
aʋan at̪a്t̪aɾam kaɾuɳajum at̪a്t̪aɾam saŋa്kaʈaʋum kaൊɳa്ʈa് n̪iraɲa്ɲu
kaɳa്ɳuniːr maŋa്ŋija n̪iɾaːʃajaോʈe kaʈʰinamaːja ʋaːka്kukaɭil
ɖa്ɾai̯ʋar maɖʱusuːd̪anan iŋa്ŋane paraɲa്ɲu
krɨʂa്ɳan
iː balaɦiːnat̪a n̪iŋa്ŋaɭe eŋa്ŋane piʈikuːʈi eʋiʈe n̪ina്n̪aːɳa് n̪iːɾuraʋakaɭ
ɖʱiːɾarka്ka് laɟa്ɟaːkaɾamaːja apakiːrt̪a്t̪ikaɾamaːja kuɻapa്pam
puɳa്jat̪a്t̪inṯe paːt̪a oɻiʋaːka്kaɳaോ ala്la arɟun
balaɦiːnat̪ajil n̪ina്n̪a് n̪iŋa്ŋaɭet̪a്t̪ana്n̪e ʋilaka്kuka at̪a് t͡ʃaൊʋa്ʋa
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe jaോd̪a്ɖʱaːʋinṯe peːɾa് bʱiːɾut̪a്ʋam t̪aɭa്ɭika്kaɭajuka
uɳaɾuka n̪iː t̪ana്n̪e aːkuka eɻuna്n̪eːlka്kuː n̪inṯe ʃat̪a്ɾuka്kaɭuʈe baːɖʱa
arɟa്ɟunan
jud̪a്ɖʱat̪a്t̪il ɲaːn eŋa്ŋane ʂaːfa്ṯṯukaɭ upajaോɡit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് ʋeʈiʋaja്ka്kum
bʱiːʂa്maɾeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaോ ala്leŋa്kil d̪a്ɾaോɳaneka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaോ ɦeː t̪alaʋaneː
ɾaɳa്ʈupeːɾum aːɾaːɖʱanajuɭa്ɭaʋaɾaോ ɾaɳa്ʈupeːɾum maːna്jaɾaːja puɾuʂana്maːɾaോ
bʱika്ʂaka്kaːɾanṯe apa്pam kaൊɳa്ʈa് ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪at̪aːɳa് n̪ala്lat̪a്
n̪ama്maɭ ɟiːʋanaോʈe sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾaോʈaൊpa്pam
samrɨd̪a്ɖʱamaːja ʋiɾuna്n̪il aʋaɾuʈe ɾaka്t̪am ɾut͡ʃika്kuna്n̪at̪ineːka്kaːɭ
kuṯṯakaɾamaːji at̪iɟiːʋika്kuka
aːɦa് at̪a് maോʃamaːjiɾuna്n̪aോaːrka്karijaːmaːkumena്n̪a്
ʋika്ʈar ala്leŋa്kil iʋiʈe paɾaːɟajapa്peʈa്ʈu
aʋar d̪eːʂa്jat̪a്t̪aോʈe n̪ama്me n̪eːɾiʈuma്paോɭ
aːɾuʈe maɾaɳam ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪e bʱajapa്peʈut̪a്t̪una്n̪u
n̪aʂa്ʈapa്peʈa്ʈa saɦat̪aːpat̪a്t̪il samʃajaŋa്ŋaɭ ʋalit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeriɲa്ɲu
enṯe t͡ʃina്t̪akaɭaʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱat̪iɾiʋa്
ɲaːn eːṯṯaʋum baɦumaːnika്kuna്n̪a ʋaɻikaːʈa്ʈijaːja n̪ina്n̪aോʈa്
ɲaːn upad̪eːʃika്kaːn paʈʰika്kaʈa്ʈe
saŋa്kaʈam ena്t̪a് maːṯṯumena്n̪a് enika്karijila്la
aːt̪a്maːʋileːka്kum ina്d̪a്ɾijat̪a്t̪ileːka്kum kat̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
ɲaːn bʱuːmijile ʋela്luʋiɭika്kapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪a t̪alaʋanaːjiɾuna്n̪uʋeŋa്kil
oɾu d̪ai̯ʋamiʋa aʋiʈe paോji
saɲa്ɟaja
aŋa്ŋane arɟa്ɟunan ɦrɨd̪ajanaːt̪ʰanaോʈa് paraɲa്ɲu
pina്n̪e n̪eʈuʋiːrpa്piʈa്ʈu ɲaːn jud̪a്ɖʱam t͡ʃeja്jila്la apa്paോɭ mau̯nam paːlit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
aːrd̪a്ɾamaːja puɲa്t͡ʃiɾijaോʈe ɦeː bʱaɾat̪a
ɾaːɟakumaːɾan n̪iɾaːʃanaːji kaɾajuma്paോɭ aː aːt̪it̪ʰeːjaɾe
krɨʂa്ɳan d̪iʋa്jaʋaːka്jat̪a്t̪il ut̪a്t̪aɾam paraɲa്ɲu
krɨʂa്ɳan
d̪uɦkʰam uɳa്ʈaːkaːn paːʈila്laːt̪a്t̪iʈat̪a്t̪a് n̪iː d̪uɦkʰika്kuna്n̪u n̪iː samsaːɾika്kuka
ɟa്ɲaːnamila്laːt̪a്t̪a ʋaːka്kukaɭ bud̪a്ɖʱijuɭa്ɭaʋarka്ka് ʋeːɳa്ʈi
ɟiːʋit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾejum maɾika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾejum oːrt̪a്t̪a് ʋilapika്kaɾut̪a്
ɲaːnaോ n̪iːjaോ iʋaɾil aːɾumala്la
oɾika്kalum uɳa്ʈaːjiɾuna്n̪ila്la oɾika്kalum uɳa്ʈaːkila്la
ena്n̪eːka്kum ena്n̪ena്n̪eːka്kumaːji
ela്laːm ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u epa്paോɻum ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u manuʂa്janṯe fa്ɾejimileːka്ka്
ʃai̯ʃaʋaʋum jau̯ʋanaʋum pa്ɾaːjaʋum ʋaɾuma്paോɭ
at̪inaːl eɻuna്n̪eːlka്kalum kiʈaka്kalum ʋaɾuː
maṯṯuɭa്ɭaʋajuʈejum maṯṯu ɟiːʋanṯejum
at̪a് ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭ arijuna്n̪u bʱajapa്peʈeːɳa്ʈat̪ila്la it̪a് asa്ʋasa്t̪ʰamaːka്kuna്n̪u 
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ina്d̪a്ɾijaɟiːʋit̪am ɡʱaʈakaŋa്ŋaɭaോʈa് aːʋeːʃabʱaɾit̪amaːɳa്
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭka്ka് t͡ʃuːʈum t̪aɳupa്pum saŋa്kaʈaŋa്ŋaɭum sana്t̪aോʂaŋa്ŋaɭum kaൊɳa്ʈuʋaɾuna്n̪u
it̪a് ɦa്ɾasa്ʋaʋum maːṯṯaːʋuna്n̪at̪umaːɳa് saɦika്kuka ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
bud̪a്ɖʱijuɭa്ɭa kaɾaʈi paോle t͡ʃalika്kaːt̪a്t̪a aːt̪a്maːʋa്
ʃaka്t̪aʋum sa്t̪ʰiɾaʋumaːja ʃaːna്t̪at̪ajuɭa്ɭa aːt̪a്maːʋa്
d̪uɦkʰam sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kukajum sana്t̪aോʂika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u
maɾika്kaːt̪a്t̪a ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪il ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u uɭa്ɭat̪a്
oɾika്kalum n̪irt̪a്t̪aːn kaɻijila്la ala്laːt̪a്t̪at̪a്
n̪ilanilka്kila്la ɾaɳa്ʈinṯejum iː sat̪a്jam kaːɳaːn
apakaʈat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് piɾiɲa്ɲat̪a് aʋaɾaːɳaോ
n̪iɻalil n̪ina്n̪uɭa്ɭa pad̪aːrt̪a്t̪ʰam n̪aʃipa്pika്kaːnaːʋaːt̪a്t̪a
n̪iː paʈʰika്kuː ɟiːʋit̪am ela്laːʋaɾilum ɟiːʋan pakaɾuna്n̪at̪aːɳa്
at̪ina് eʋiʈejum oɾu t̪aɾat̪a്t̪ilum kaɻijila്la
eŋa്ŋanejeŋa്kilum kurajukajaോ t̪uʈaɾukajaോ maːṯṯukajaോ t͡ʃeja്juka
ena്n̪aːl at̪a് arijika്kuna്n̪a iː ka്ʂaɳikamaːja fa്ɾejimukaɭka്kaːji
aːt̪a്maːʋinaൊpa്pam maɾaɳamila്laːt̪a്t̪a anan̪a്t̪amaːja anan̪a്t̪amaːja
aʋar n̪aʃika്kuna്n̪u aʋar n̪aʃika്kaʈa്ʈe ɾaːɟakumaːɾaː jud̪a്ɖʱam t͡ʃeja്juka
ɲaːn oɾu manuʂa്jane kaൊn̪a്n̪iɾika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪u parajuna്n̪aʋan
it̪aː ɲaːn kaൊla്lapa്peʈa്ʈu ena്n̪a് t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋan aʋa ɾaɳa്ʈum
ona്n̪umarijila്la ɟiːʋana് kaൊla്laːnaːʋila്la ɟiːʋan kaൊla്lapa്peʈa്ʈiʈa്ʈila്la
oɾika്kalum aːt̪a്maːʋa് ɟanit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiʈa്ʈila്la aːt̪a്maːʋa് oɾika്kalum ila്laːt̪aːkum
oɾika്kalum samajamaːjiɾuna്n̪ila്la aŋa്ŋanejala്la aʋasaːnaʋum t̪uʈaka്kaʋum sa്ʋapa്n̪aŋa്ŋaɭaːɳa്
ɟanan̪amila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪um maɾaɳamila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪um maːṯṯamila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪um aːt̪a്maːʋaːji ena്n̪eːka്kum n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪u
maɾaɳam at̪ine sa്parʃit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiʈa്ʈila്la maɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪aːji t̪aോn̪a്n̪umeŋa്kilum
at̪a് ka്ʂiːɳamila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪um sa്ʋajam n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪at̪um aːrka്karijaːm
anaʃa്ʋaɾamaːja n̪aːʃamila്laːt̪a്t̪aŋa്ŋanejaːjiɾika്kum
parajuka ɲaːn oɾu manuʂa്jane kaൊn̪a്n̪aോ at̪aോ kaൊla്laːn pa്ɾeːɾipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaോ
ala്la oɾuʋan kiʈaka്kuma്paോɭ ena്n̪apaോle
aʋanṯe ɟiːrɳit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa ʋasa്t̪a്ɾaŋa്ŋaɭ d̪uːɾejaːji
put̪ijaʋa eʈut̪a്t̪a് parajuna്n̪u
iʋa ɲaːn ina്n̪a് ɖʱaɾika്kum
aŋa്ŋane aːt̪a്maːʋinaːl sa്t̪ʰaːpika്kuna്n̪u
laɡʱuʋaːji at̪inṯe maːmsa ʋasa്t̪a്ɾam
anan̪a്t̪aɾaːʋakaːʃamaːji kaʈana്n̪upaോkuna്n̪u
put̪ut̪aːji oɾu t̪aːmasasa്t̪ʰalam
ɲaːn n̪ina്n̪aോʈu parajuna്n̪u aːjuɖʱaŋa്ŋaɭ ɟiːʋanil et̪a്t̪una്n̪ila്la
aɡa്n̪iɟa്ʋaːla at̪ine kat̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪ila്la ʋeɭa്ɭat̪a്t̪ina് kiːɻaʈaka്kaːn kaɻijila്la
ʋaɾaɳa്ʈa kaːṯṯum at̪ine uɳaŋa്ŋuna്n̪ila്la abʱeːd̪a്jamaːja
pa്ɾaʋeːʃika്kaːt̪a്t̪a aːka്ɾamika്kapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪a paɾika്keːlka്kaːt̪a്t̪a t̪aൊʈa്ʈukuːʈaːt̪a്t̪a
anaʃa്ʋaɾan ela്laːm et̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːɾuna്n̪a sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪ajuɭa്ɭa urapa്puɭa്ɭa
ad̪rɨʃa്jamaːja ʋiʋaɾaɳaːt̪iːt̪amaːja ʋaːka്kaːl
anijana്t̪a്ɾit̪amaːji t͡ʃina്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃu epa്paോɻum ela്laːm t̪ana്n̪e
aŋa്ŋanejaːɳa് aːt̪a്maːʋa് pa്ɾakʰa്jaːpit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪at̪a് apa്paോɭ n̪inaka്ka് eŋa്ŋanejaːʋum
at̪a് ariɲa്ɲukaൊɳa്ʈa്  d̪uɦkʰika്kaːt̪iɾika്kuma്paോɭ d̪uɦkʰika്kaɳaോ
aː manuʂa്jan put̪ut̪aːji maɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuʋena്n̪u keːʈa്ʈaːl eŋa്ŋane
n̪aʋaɟaːt̪anaːja manuʂa്janepa്paോle ipa്paോɻum ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪a manuʂa്jan 
at̪eː n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪a aːt̪a്maːʋa്  n̪iː kaɾajumaോ
ɟanan̪at̪a്t̪inṯe aʋasaːnam maɾaɳamaːɳa് maɾaɳat̪a്t̪inṯe aʋasaːnam
ɟanan̪am it̪a് n̪ijamika്kapa്peʈa്ʈat̪aːɳa് n̪iː d̪uɦkʰika്kuna്n̪u
ʃaka്t̪anaːja bʱuɟat̪a്t̪inṯe t̪alaʋan ena്t̪a് sambʱaʋika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪at̪ina്
ala്laːt̪e sambʱaʋika്kaːt̪a്t̪at̪a് eːt̪aːɳa് ɟanan̪am
ɟiːʋaɟaːlaŋa്ŋaɭ ɡa്ɾaɦika്kaːt̪e ʋaɾuna്n̪u maɾaɳam
ɡa്ɾaɦika്kaːt̪e ʋaɾuna്n̪u aʋaja്ka്kiʈajil ɟiːʋikaɭ manasa്silaːka്kuna്n̪u
pa്ɾija ɾaːɟakumaːɾaː it̪il ena്t̪aːɳa് d̪uɦkʰakaɾamaːjat̪a്
at̪a്bʱut̪am aːɡa്ɾaɦam t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kaːn
samsaːɾika്kaːn pa്ɾajaːsam samʃajam
ʋit͡ʃit̪a്ɾaʋum n̪aːʋinaോʈa് samʋad̪ika്kaːn mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪um
oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪arka്kum misa്ṯṯika് keːɭʋi
manuʂa്jan it̪aൊn̪a്n̪um t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kuna്n̪ila്la ena്t̪aൊɾu at̪a്bʱut̪amaːɳit̪a്
kaːɳukajum parajukajum keːɭka്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juma്paോɭ
ela്laː ɟiːʋaɟaːlaŋa്ŋaɭka്kum uɭa്ɭile iː ɟiːʋit̪am enṯe ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
d̪aോʂat̪a്t̪inapa്puram marajuna്n̪u n̪iː kaʂa്ʈapa്peʈaːn put͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰika്kuna്n̪u pina്n̪e
saɦika്kaːn kaɻijaːt̪a്t̪at̪ina് n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe bʱaːɡam t͡ʃeja്juka
n̪inṯe n̪aːmam oːrt̪a്t̪iɾika്kuka ʋiraja്ka്kaɾut̪a്
oɾu aːjaോɖʱana aːt̪a്maːʋine t̪aɭart̪a്t̪aːn it̪ilum mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪aൊn̪a്n̪um ila്la
n̪ijamaːnusrɨt̪amaːja jud̪a്ɖʱat̪a്t̪eːka്kaːɭ jaോd̪a്ɖʱaːʋina് sana്t̪aോʂam
jud̪a്ɖʱat̪a്t̪inṯe sana്t̪aോʂam aːrka്ka് ʋaɾuna്n̪u  ipa്paോɭ ʋaɾuna്n̪at̪upaോle
maɦat̪a്ʋaʋum n̪a്jaːjaʋum ana്ʋeːʂika്kapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪a aʋanuʋeːɳa്ʈi t̪uraka്kuna്n̪u
ɦeʋinileːka്kuɭa്ɭa oɾu kaʋaːʈam paka്ʂeː n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ oɻiʋaːka്kukajaːɳeŋa്kil

aʋanṯe bʱau̯mika ʋeːd̪anakaɭuʈe aʋasaːnaʋum ɾaോɡaʃaːna്t̪ijum
bʱaɾika്kuna്n̪a it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰaːʃaka്t̪i aːt̪a്maːʋine ʃaːna്t̪amaːka്kuna്n̪at̪inaːl
bʱaɾaɳamila്laːt̪a്t̪aʋanṯe aːt̪a്maːʋa് aʋanuɭa്ɭat̪ala്la
aʋanu t̪ana്n̪epa്paṯṯi ariʋila്la ila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪a്
ʃaːna്t̪at̪a eŋa്ŋane ʋaɭaɾuna്n̪u opa്pam at̪a് aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kuna്n̪u
aʋan eʋiʈe n̪ina്n̪aːɳa് sana്t̪aോʂam pa്ɾat̪iːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪at̪a്
manasa്sa്
at̪a് art̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪inṯe pa്ɾakaʈanaŋa്ŋaɭ pina്t̪uʈaɾaːn sa്ʋajam n̪alkuna്n̪u
at̪inṯe ɟa്ɲaːnat̪a്t̪inṯe t͡ʃuka്kaːn n̪aോka്kuna്n̪u
opa്pam t͡ʃuɻalika്kaːṯṯinṯe t̪iɾamaːlakaɭil oɾu kapa്pal paോle oːʈika്kuna്n̪u
t̪akart͡ʃa്t͡ʃajileːka്kum maɾaɳat̪a്t̪ileːka്kum aʋanaോʈaൊpa്pam maːt̪a്ɾam maɦaːnaːja ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
aːɾuʈe ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭ ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭaːl sa്ʋaːɖʱiːnika്kapa്peʈuna്n̪ila്la 
t̪anṯe jaɟamaːnan̪umaːji maːt̪a്ɾam
t̪ikaɲa്ɲa ɟa്ɲaːnam kaːɳika്kuna്n̪u ena്t̪aːɳa് ard̪a്ɖʱaɾaːt̪a്ɾiana്ɖʱakaːɾam
pa്ɾakaːʃamila്laːt̪a്t̪a aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭka്ka് uɳarn̪a്n̪iɾika്kuna്n̪a d̪iʋasam pa്ɾakaːʃika്kuna്n̪u
aʋanṯe ʋa്jaka്t̪amaːja n̪aോʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് uɳarn̪a്n̪iɾika്kuna്n̪a d̪iʋasam paോle t̪aോn̪a്n̪una്n̪u
ɾaːt̪a്ɾi arijapa്peʈuna്n̪at̪a് aɟa്ɲat̪ajuʈe kanat̪a്t̪a ɾaːt̪a്ɾi
aʋanṯe jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa kaɳa്ɳukaɭileːka്ka് aŋa്ŋanejaːɳa് ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱan
samud̪a്ɾam paോle d̪iʋasam t̪aോrum sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kuna്n̪u
oɾika്kalum kaʋiɲa്ɲaൊɻukaːt̪a്t̪a ela്laː d̪eːʃaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪um ʋeɭa്ɭapa്paൊka്kam
at̪inṯe at̪irt̪a്t̪i ɾeːkʰa t͡ʃaːʈuna്n̪ila്la ʋiʈa്ʈupaോkuna്n̪ila്la

at̪upaോle t̪ikaɲa്ɲa ona്n̪aːɳa് aʋanṯe aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe samud̪a്ɾat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka്

aʋaɾuʈe aːd̪aɾaːɲa്ɟali eːṯṯuʋaːŋa്ŋuna്n̪u paka്ʂeː kaʈal aʋaʃeːʂika്kuna്n̪u
at̪e maːmsat̪a്t̪inṯe n̪ukam kuʈaɲa്ɲukaɭajuna്n̪aʋan

aɦaŋa്kaːɾat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് abʱiniʋeːʃat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് sa്ʋajam ena്n̪a paːpat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a്

aː aʋasaːna ɡʱaʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪ilet̪a്t̪uma്paോɭ aʋan aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kuna്n̪iʈat̪a്t̪a് ɟiːʋika്kuka

srɨʂa്ʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a് ʋiʃa്ɾamika്kuna്n̪a ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪at̪a് ɲaːn

pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ maɳa്ɳaːɳa് enṯe sat̪a്t̪ajala്la pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijaːɳa്
uɭpa്peʈaːt̪e uɳa്ʈaːka്ki# ɲaːn iŋa്ŋane abʱinajika്kumena്n̪a് aːrka്karijaːm
pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijaːl bana്ɖʱika്kapa്peʈaːt̪e pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪i aʋane bana്ɖʱika്kuna്n̪ila്la
kuːʈaːt̪e paɻaja ela്laː ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱana്maːɾejum manasa്silaːka്kuna്n̪u
maോt͡ʃanam t̪eːʈi pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃu n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuka
kaɻiɲa്ɲa n̪aːɭukaɭil n̪inṯe pit̪aːka്kana്maːr t͡ʃeja്t̪at̪upaോle
ama്paɾapa്paോʈe n̪iː parajuna്n̪u muma്pa് t͡ʃaോd̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪aːɳa്
ɡaːjakaɾaːlum ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭaːlum ena്t̪aːɳa് pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪i
pina്n̪e ena്t̪a് n̪iʂa്ka്ɾijat̪a്ʋam it̪a് ɲaːn n̪ina്n̪e paʈʰipa്pika്kaːm
kuːʈaːt̪e eːt̪a് ɟaോlijaːɳa് ɾaka്ʂika്keːɳa്ʈat̪ena്n̪a് ariɲa്ɲukaൊɳa്ʈa് n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ paʈʰika്kum
aːʋaʃa്jaŋa്ŋaɭ oɾaːɭ aː muːna്n̪eɳa്ɳam ʃaɾijaːji ɖʱa്jaːnika്kaɳam
t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪ut͡ʃeja്juna്n̪ila്lala്laːt̪aːka്kuna്n̪u iʋiʈe
muɭa്ɭum iɾuʈa്ʈum n̪iraɲa്ɲa paːt̪a kaːɳuna്n̪aʋan
pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anam eŋa്ŋane ʋiʃa്ɾamam ʋiʃa്ɾama pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anam  aʋan
aʋanṯe t̪aɾam mad̪a്ɖʱa്jeː eːṯṯaʋum ɟa്ɲaːni aʋanu sat̪a്jamuɳa്ʈa്
aʋan n̪ana്n̪aːji pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u abʱinajika്kuna്n̪u ala്leŋa്kil ʋiʃa്ɾamika്kuna്n̪u maോt͡ʃipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
aʋanṯe ela്laː srɨʂa്ʈikaɭilum aːɡa്ɾaɦat̪a്t̪inṯe kut̪a്t̪ukaɭil n̪ina്n̪a്
sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋeɭut̪a്t̪a t̪iːjaːl pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijil ʃud̪a്ɖʱamaːji
ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭ aː manuʂa്jane ɟa്ɲaːni ena്n̪u ʋiɭika്kuna്n̪u at̪a്t̪aɾat̪a്t̪iluɭa്ɭa ona്n̪a്
karma്mapʰalam t̪a്jaɟit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് epa്paോɻum samt̪rɨpa്t̪ijaോʈe
epa്paോɻum sa്ʋajam samt̪rɨpa്t̪anaːɳa് aʋan pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kukajaːɳeŋa്kil
aʋanṯe pa്ɾat̪a്jeːka aːt̪a്maːʋine kaɭaŋa്kapa്peʈut̪a്t̪una്n̪a ona്n̪um t͡ʃeja്jaɾut̪a്
eːt̪a്  bʱajaʋum pa്ɾat̪iːka്ʂajum upeːka്ʂika്kuka  sa്ʋajam kiːɻaʈaka്kuka 
baːɦa്jamaːja pa്ɾeːɾaɳa n̪iɾasika്kuna്n̪u  ʋaɻaŋa്ŋuna്n̪u
ʃaɾiːɾat̪a്t̪ina് ʃaɾiːɾamala്laːt̪e maṯṯaൊn̪a്n̪um aːʋaʃa്jamila്la ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
ela്laː paːpaŋa്ŋaɭka്kiʈajilum paːpaɾaɦit̪an t̪ula്ja ʃaːna്t̪at̪ajaോʈe
sambʱaʋit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːka്kaːʋuna്n̪at̪a് sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kuna്n̪u d̪uɦkʰat̪a്t̪aːl anaŋa്ŋaːt̪e
sana്t̪aോʂat̪a്t̪aːl t͡ʃalika്kaːt̪e asuːjapa്peʈaːt̪e at̪ut̪ana്n̪e
n̪ala്lat̪um t͡ʃiːt̪a്t̪ajumaːja bʱaːɡa്jaŋa്ŋaɭil ipa്paോɭ bana്ɖʱika്kapa്peʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪u
karma്ma bana്ɖʱat̪a്t̪aːl ala്la paka്ʂeː aŋa്ŋanejuɭa്ɭa oɾaːɭuʈe
aːɾuʈe aːɡa്ɾaɦam ila്laːt̪aːji aːɾuʈe aːt̪a്maːʋa് ʋimaോt͡ʃit̪amaːɳa്
aːɾuʈe ɦrɨd̪ajam sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪il pat̪iɲa്ɲiɾika്kuna്n̪u  aŋa്ŋanejuɭa്ɭaʋanṯe
aʋan t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪a ɟaോli t̪a്jaːɡat̪a്t̪inṯe pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijaːɳa്
at̪a് puːrɳa്ɳamaːjum t͡ʃaːɾat̪a്t̪ileːka്kum pukajileːka്kum kaʈana്n̪upaോkuna്n̪u
balipiːʈʰat̪a്t̪il d̪aɦipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu apa്paോɭ ela്laːm d̪ai̯ʋam
ba്ɾaɦa്maʋum n̪eja്jum ɖʱaːna്jaʋumaːɳa് jaːɡam
ba്ɾaɦa്mamaːɳaോ aɡa്n̪ijaːɳa് ba്ɾaɦa്mam at̪a് bʱaka്ʂika്kuna്n̪a maːmsamaːɳa്
ba്ɾaɦa്mamaːɳa് ba്ɾaɦa്mat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് aʋan et̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːɾuna്n̪u
at̪a്t̪aɾam oːfiːsil aːɾaːɳa് ba്ɾaɦa്mat̪a്t̪e ɖʱa്jaːnika്kuna്n̪at̪a്
d̪ai̯ʋaŋa്ŋaɭe seːʋika്kuna്n̪a t͡ʃila ʋaോʈa്ʈarmaːɾuɳa്ʈa്
maːmsat̪a്t̪aോʈum jaːɡapiːʈʰat̪a്t̪aോʈum kuːʈija pukajum ena്n̪aːl maṯṯu t͡ʃilat̪a്
aːr suːka്ʂa്mamaːja t̪iː kat̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് ʃud̪a്ɖʱamaːja aːt͡ʃaːɾam n̪aʈat̪a്t̪una്n̪u
aːɾaːɖʱanaː iʂa്ʈat̪a്t̪aോʈe aʋajil n̪ina്n̪a്
kaɳa്ʈinṯe ʋeɭut̪a്t̪a ɟa്ʋaːlajil aːɾaːɳa് d̪aɦipa്pika്kuna്n̪at̪a്
ina്d̪a്ɾijat̪a്t̪inṯe aːnan̪a്d̪am kaɳa്ɳinum kaːt̪inumuɭa്ɭa aːnan̪a്d̪am
aːrd̪a്ɾamaːja samsaːɾaʋum paːʈa്ʈinṯe ʃaba്d̪aʋum upeːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u
sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪inṯe d̪iːpam kaൊɳa്ʈa് t̪iː kat̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾum
oɾu maraɲa്ɲiɾika്kuna്n̪a balipiːʈʰat̪a്t̪il aːnan̪a്d̪am kat̪a്t̪ika്kuka
juʋat̪a്ʋat̪a്t̪inṯejum sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inṯejum sana്t̪aോʂam upeːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u
aʋiʈe t̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe sama്pat̪a്t̪a് arpa്pika്kaːn kiʈaka്kuna്n̪aʋar
aʋaɾuʈe t̪apasa്sa് ɖʱa്jaːnam bʱaka്t̪i
t͡ʃuɾuɭukaɭuʈe aʋaɾuʈe urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa ʋaːjana aʋaɾuʈe ai̯t̪iɦa്jaŋa്ŋaɭ
n̪iːɳa്ʈa t̪apasa്sukaൊɳa്ʈa് ʋeːd̪anaːɟanakamaːji n̪eːʈijat̪a്
n̪iʃa്ʃaba്d̪amaːja t̪a്jaːɡam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪aʋaɾum
t͡ʃina്t̪ajuʈe ɟa്ʋaːla t̪iːṯṯaːn aʋaɾuʈe ʃa്ʋaːsam ʋaɾaja്ka്kuka
ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪e ujaɾat̪a്t̪il t͡ʃalipa്pika്kaːn at̪a് ʃa്ʋasika്kuka
pa്ɾaʋeːʃika്kuna്n̪a oːɾaോ ʋaːjuʋinṯejum ʋenṯeːɟa് n̪ijana്t̪a്ɾika്kuna്n̪u
aːt̪a്maːʋine saɦaːjika്kaːt̪a്t̪a oɾu n̪eʈuʋiːrpa്pa് kaʈana്n̪upaോkaːt̪iɾika്kaːn
d̪inampa്ɾat̪i aːʋaʃa്jaŋa്ŋaɭ n̪iʂeːɖʱika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾum
jaːɡapiːʈʰat̪a്t̪inṯe t̪iːɟa്ʋaːlajil ɟiːʋan ʋaja്ka്kuka
ʃaɾiːɾam kat̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u at̪aː iʋajela്laːm suːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u
ʋaɻipaːʈa് aʋar kaൊn̪a്n̪at̪upaോle
iɾakaɭ ela്laːm at̪uʋaɻi ʋaɭaɾe paːpam ila്laːt̪aːka്kuna്n̪u
at̪e anaʃa്ʋaɾamaːja bʱaka്ʂaɳam kaɻika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾum
at̪a്t̪aɾam t̪a്jaːɡam upeːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋileːka്ka്
leːka്ka് d̪i aɳenɖimɡa് ena്n̪aːl aʋanu ʋeːɳa്ʈi
t̪a്jaːɡamila്la aʋana് bʱaːɡamaോ bʱaːɡamaോ bʱaːɡamaോ ila്la
ina്n̪at̪a്t̪e laോkat̪a്t̪il paോlum aʋan eŋa്ŋane paŋa്kiʈaɳam
maṯṯaൊn̪a്n̪a് n̪inṯe ʋaɾijuʈe maɦat̪a്ʋamuɳa്ʈaോ
iː ʋaɻipaːʈukaɭela്laːm ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋinṯe d̪rɨʂa്ʈijil
ʋa്jaːpika്kukajum amɡiːkaɾika്kapa്peʈukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u manasa്silaːka്kuka
ela്laːm pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijiluːʈe muna്n̪aോʈa്ʈa് paോkuna്n̪u it̪ariɲa്ɲat̪ina്
n̪iː samʃajat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് muka്t̪anaːkum jaːɡam
maɦat̪a്t̪aːja sama്maːnaŋa്ŋaɭeːka്kaːɭ mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a് eːt̪a് ariʋaːɳa് pa്ɾat̪ipʰalam n̪alkuna്n̪at̪a്
sama്pat̪a്t̪a് ʋaːɡa്d̪aːnam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u sama്maːnaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe muːla്jam mut̪aloː enṯe ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
n̪alkuna്n̪a manasa്silaːɳa് seːʋika്kuna്n̪a it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰaːʃaka്t̪i
bʱaka്t̪ijaːl ʃaka്t̪amaːja t̪iɾat͡ʃa്t͡ʃil ʋaɻijaːɳa് iʋa n̪eːʈijat̪a്
sat̪a്jam kaːɳuna്n̪aʋaɾuʈe eɭija ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱajaːl
at̪a് paʈʰipa്pika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juka sat̪a്jam ariɲa്ɲaːl n̪inṯe ɦrɨd̪ajam inijila്la
t̪eṯṯa് kaൊɳa്ʈa് ʋeːd̪anika്kum kaːɾaɳam sat̪a്jam kaːɳika്kum
n̪iː ena്n̪epa്paോle ela്laːm n̪inaka്ku kiːɻa്peʈut̪a്t̪ijiɾika്kuna്n̪u
maːt̪a്ɾamala്la paːɳa്ɖuʋinṯe put̪a്ɾan n̪iː eːṯṯaʋum maോʃamaːjiɾuna്n̪u
ela്laː t̪eṯṯukaːɾil n̪ina്n̪um sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪inṯe iː n̪a്jaːjamaːja kapa്pal
n̪ina്n̪e suɾaka്ʂit̪amaːjum kaʈalina് kuruke ʋaɾaɳa്ʈat̪aːka്kum
n̪inṯe at̪ika്ɾamaŋa്ŋaɭil ɟa്ʋalika്kuna്n̪a ɟa്ʋaːla paോle
t͡ʃaːɾamaːji muŋa്ŋuna്n̪at̪a് ʋaɾe ina്ɖʱanam bʱaka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u
at̪inaːl t͡ʃaːɾat̪a്t̪ina് arɟa്ɟunaː ona്n̪umila്la
ariʋinṯe ɟa്ʋaːla pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anaŋa്ŋaɭe paːɻaːka്kuna്n̪u
at̪upaോlaൊɾu pa്juːɾifajar ila്la
iː laോkat̪a്t̪il muɻuʋanum at̪a് ana്ʋeːʂika്kuna്n̪aʋanum
at̪a് kaɳa്ʈet̪a്t̪um  paɾipuːrɳa്ɳamaːji ʋaɭarn̪a്n̪at̪a്  t̪ana്n̪ilt̪a്t̪ana്n̪e
ʋiʃa്ʋasika്kuna്n̪u aːt̪a്maːʋa് ʋaɾuma്paോɭ aʋan at̪a് sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kuna്n̪u
sa്ʋajam jaɟamaːnan̪aːji sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪aോʈa് t͡ʃeːrn̪a്n̪unilka്kuna്n̪u ʋaɾuna്n̪u
ariʋa് kai̯ʋaʃam ʋaja്ka്kuka  ujarn̪a്n̪a samaːɖʱaːnat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka്
paɾamamaːja ʋiʃa്ɾamam ena്n̪aːl paʈʰipa്pika്kaːt̪a്t̪aʋar
puːrɳa്ɳa ʋiʃa്ʋaːsamila്laːt̪a്t̪aʋaɾum bʱajapa്peʈuna്n̪aʋaɾum
ʂenṯa് t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u iʋiʈejaോ maṯṯeʋiʈejaോ samaːɖʱaːnamila്la
samʃajika്kuna്n̪aʋarka്ka് pa്ɾat̪iːka്ʂajaോ sana്t̪aോʂamaോ ila്la
sa്ʋajam uɭka്kaൊɭa്ɭuna്n̪aʋan samʃajaniʋaːɾaɳam t͡ʃeja്t̪u
sa്ʋajam seːʋanat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪um aːt̪a്maːʋine pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭil n̪ina്n̪um akaṯṯuna്n̪u
pa്ɾabud̪a്ɖʱat̪ajum ʋimaോt͡ʃanaʋum enṯe ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ aʋane ʋalaja്ka്kila്la murit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaʃeːʂam uʈan
ɟa്ɲaːnat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋaːɭukaൊɳa്ʈa് bʱaɾat̪aput̪a്ɾaː
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ɦrɨd̪ajamiʈipa്pukaɭe bana്ɖʱipa്pika്kuna്n̪a iː samʃajam bana്ɖʱanam piɭart̪a്t̪uka
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe aɟa്ɲat̪ajil n̪ina്n̪a് ɟanit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a് ɖʱai̯ɾa്jaʋum ɟa്ɲaːnaʋum aːjiɾika്kuka
ena്n̪aോʈukuːʈe ʋajalil n̪ina്n̪et̪a്t̪ana്n̪eː t̪aɾika eɻuna്n̪eːlka്kuː
iʋiʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam  bʱaɡaʋad̪a് ɡiːt̪ajuʈe
ɟa്ɲaːnajaോɡa് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil ariʋinṯe mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam ʋi
arɟa്ɟunan
ena്n̪aːlum krɨʂa്ɳaː oɾu samajat̪a്t̪a് n̪iː sa്t̪ut̪ika്kum
pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭuʈe ʋaɭart͡ʃa്t͡ʃa maṯṯaൊɾu samajat̪a്t̪a്
ɟaോlijiluːʈe seːʋanam iʋa ɾaɳa്ʈum ʋa്jaka്t̪amaːji parajuna്n̪u
eːt̪aːɳa് n̪ala്la ʋaɻi
krɨʂa്ɳan
ɟaോlikaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് n̪irt̪a്t̪aːn
ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱijaോʈe pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪um n̪ala്lat̪aːɳa്
sukʰamaːɳa് ɾaɳa്ʈum paɾamamaːja aːnan̪a്d̪at̪a്t̪ileːka്kuɭa്ɭa peɾumaːṯṯaʋum
ena്n̪aːl iː ɾaɳa്ʈil eːṯṯaʋum n̪ala്la ʋaɻi aʋanṯet̪aːɳa്
ɖʱarma്maniʂa്ʈʰajaോʈe pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋan t̪aʈajuna്n̪ila്la
at̪aːɳa് jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa n̪iɾaːkaːɾan urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪um sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪ajuɭa്ɭat̪um
aːɾaːɳa്  ona്n̪um ana്ʋeːʂika്kuna്n̪ila്la ona്n̪um n̪iɾasika്kuna്n̪u  t̪eɭiʋil ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
et̪iɾaːɭikaɭka്ket̪iɾe# oː ɖʱiːɾanaːja ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪iluːʈe at̪a്t̪aɾam ela്laː pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭil n̪ina്n̪um laɡʱuʋaːji t̪akarka്kuna്n̪u
aʋar ɾaɳa്ʈupeːɾaːji put̪ija paɳa്ɖit̪an samsaːɾika്kuna്n̪u
iː samkʰa്jajum iː jaോɡaʋum ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭka്ka് arijaːm
bʱart̪a്t̪aːka്kana്maːr ɾaɳa്ʈinṯejum sa്ʋarɳa്ɳa pʰalam parit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeʈuka്kuna്n̪u
saːmkʰa്jana്maːr et̪a്t̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːɾuna്n̪a ujarn̪a്n̪a ʋiʃa്ɾama meːkʰala
jaോɡikaɭ n̪eːʈuna്n̪u aːɾaːɳa് iː ɾaɳa്ʈupeːɾejum ona്n̪aːji kaːɳuna്n̪at̪a്
t̪eɭiɲa്ɲa kaɳa്ɳukaɭaോʈe kaːɳuna്n̪u ena്n̪aːlum at̪a്t̪aɾam amuːrt̪a്t̪at̪a t͡ʃiːfa്
ʋalija ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱijila്laːt̪e ɟajika്kuka pa്ɾajaːsamaːɳa്
ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱijil urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃunilka്kuna്n̪aʋan sa്ʋajam bʱaɾika്kuna്n̪aʋan
ʃud̪a്ɖʱaɦrɨd̪ajan ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭuʈejum sa്ʋana്t̪at̪a്t̪inṯejum aɖʱipan
ela്laːʋaɾuʈejum paൊt̪uɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪il n̪aʂa്ʈapa്peʈa്ʈu
oɾu jaോɡaːjuka്t̪a്  aʋan oɾu ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱanaːɳa്
n̪eːɾe ba്ɾaɦa്mat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് aŋa്ŋanejaൊɾaːɭ t̪aൊʈila്la
karma്maŋa്ŋaɭuʈe kaɭaŋa്kat̪a്t̪aːl ɲaːn sa്ʋajam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪ala്la
aŋa്ŋane aʋan ʋit͡ʃaːɾika്kumsat̪a്jaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪e aːrka്ka് piʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪u
kaːɳal keːɭka്kal sa്parʃanam maɳam ena്n̪iʋajil epa്poːɭ
aʋan t̪ina്n̪una്n̪u ala്leŋa്kil paോkuna്n̪u ala്leŋa്kil ʃa്ʋasika്kuna്n̪u uraka്kam ala്leŋa്kil samsaːɾam
muruke piʈika്kukajaോ ajaʋuʋaɾut̪a്t̪ukajaോ kaɳa്ɳukaɭ t̪uraka്kukajaോ aʈaja്ka്kukajaോ t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u
ela്laːja്pa്paോɻum urapa്punalkuna്n̪u it̪a് ina്d̪a്ɾijalaോka n̪aːʈakaŋa്ŋaɭaːɳa്
ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭaːl ba്ɾaɦa്mat̪a്t̪eka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuɭa്ɭa t͡ʃina്t̪ajil pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋan
aːka്ʈil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋeːrpeʈut̪a്t̪al aːka്ʈinṯe uɭa്ɭaʈaka്kam
ina്d̪a്ɾijalaോkat̪a്t̪ina് ini aʋanṯe aːt̪a്maːʋine kaɭaŋa്kapa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːnaːʋila്la
ʋeɭa്ɭat̪a്t̪eːka്kaːɭ maːrt̪a്t̪a് inaːmalɖa് t̪aːmaɾila
ɟiːʋit̪am kaൊɳa്ʈa് ɦrɨd̪ajam kaൊɳa്ʈa് manasa്sa് kaൊɳa്ʈa് ala്la saɦaːjat̪a്t̪aːl
ela്laː paɲa്t͡ʃeːna്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭilumsa്ʋaːrt̪a്t̪ʰat̪aje ʋiʈa്ʈajaka്kuka
jaോɡikaɭ t̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭuʈe maോt͡ʃanat̪a്t̪inaːji ena്n̪um ad̪a്ɖʱa്ʋaːnika്kuna്n̪u
at̪a്t̪aɾam ʋaോʈa്ʈarmaːr karma്mapʰalam t̪a്jaɟika്kuna്n̪u
anan̪a്t̪amaːja samaːɖʱaːnam n̪eːʈuka pa്ɾat̪iɟa്ɲa t͡ʃeja്jaːt̪a്t̪aʋar abʱiniʋeːʃam keʈa്ʈaʋar
pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് pʰalam t̪eːʈi muruke piʈika്kuna്n̪u
muːrt̪a്t̪iːbʱaːʋamuɭa്ɭa muni t̪anṯe aːt̪a്maːʋinuɭa്ɭil pinʋalit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
oːɾaോ pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijilum paʈa്ʈaɳat̪a്t̪il d̪ai̯ʋat̪a്t̪epa്paോle iɾika്kuna്n̪u
oma്pat̪a് ɡeːṯṯa്‌ʋeːkaɭuɭa്ɭa# ona്n̪um t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪ila്la
oɾu karma്maʋum uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪ila്la iː laോkat̪a്t̪inṯe kart̪a്t̪aːʋa് uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪u
ɟaോlijaോ ɟaോlijaോʈuɭa്ɭa abʱiniʋeːʃamaോ ala്la
ad̪a്ɖʱa്ʋaːnat̪a്t̪inṯe pʰalat̪a്t̪inuʋeːɳa്ʈijuɭa്ɭa maോɦaʋumila്la manuʂa്janṯe sa്ʋana്t̪am
iʋajileːka്ka് t̪aɭa്ɭuna്n̪u iː laോkat̪a്t̪inṯe jaɟamaːnan
n̪ala്lat̪aോ t͡ʃiːt̪a്t̪ajaോ aːja pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ sa്ʋajam eːṯṯeʈuka്kuna്n̪u
oɾu manuʂa്janṯejum  apa്puram ʋasika്kuna്n̪u manuʂa്jaɾaːʃi iʋiʈe t̪eṯṯi
ʋiɖa്ɖʱit̪a്t̪am ariʋine iɾuʈa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪u paka്ʂeː aːrka്kuʋeːɳa്ʈi
aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe iɾuʈa്ʈine ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam pina്t̪uʈaɾuna്n̪u
ɡambʱiːɾaʋum ʋa്jaka്t̪aʋumaːja pa്ɾakaːʃam sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪e pa്ɾakaʈamaːka്kuna്n̪u
ɟa്ɲaːnasuːɾa്jan t͡ʃaൊɾijuna്n̪at̪upaോle
at̪inṯe pa്ɾabʱaːt̪akiɾaɳaŋa്ŋaɭ aʋan ipa്paോɻum ɖʱa്jaːnat̪a്t̪ilaːɳa്
aʋan ana്ʋeːʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu aʋanumaːji lajit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu aʋanil n̪ina്n̪u
pa്ɾakaːʃit̪amaːja aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭ aː ʋaɻijiluːʈe saɲa്t͡ʃaɾika്kuna്n̪u
pina്t̪iɾiɲa്ɲupaോkaːt̪a്t̪a aʋaɾuʈe paːpaŋa്ŋaɭ parana്n̪upaോji
ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪inṯe ʃaka്t̪ijaːl iː ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam aːrka്kuɳa്ʈaːkum
at̪uɭa്ɭaʋan kaːɳuna്n̪u ʋiʋeːkat̪a്t̪aോʈe kaːɳuna്n̪aʋanaോʈa്
ba്ɾaːɦa്maɳan t̪anṯe t͡ʃuɾuɭukaɭum ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱikaɭumaːji

laോkam ɟajit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu  at̪e iʋiʈe paോlum
at̪a്t̪aɾaka്kaːr t̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ʋiʃa്ʋaːsam ai̯ka്jat̪a്t̪il urapa്pika്kuka
paːpaɾaɦit̪anaːja ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋa് eːkat̪a്ʋat̪a്t̪il ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
aʋar ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋilum amit̪amaːji sana്t̪aോʂika്kaɾut̪a്
sana്t̪aോʂam n̪eːʈuna്n̪u amit̪amaːji d̪uɦkʰika്kaɾut̪a്
d̪uɦkʰam n̪eːɾiʈa്ʈu paka്ʂeː ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋil t̪ana്n̪e n̪ina്n̪u
sa്t̪ʰiɾamaːji oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪aɾum n̪ilanilka്kaʈa്ʈe rɨʂi aːɾuʈe aːt̪a്maːʋaːɳa്
t̪ana്n̪ilt̪a്t̪ana്n̪ejuɭa്ɭa baːɦa്ja sama്parka്kaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋiʈa്ʈunilka്kuna്n̪u
aːnan̪a്d̪am kaɳa്ʈet̪a്t̪una്n̪u ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋinaോʈa് bʱaka്t̪i t͡ʃeːrn̪a്n̪u
aʋanṯe aːt̪a്maːʋa് n̪it̪a്jaʃaːna്t̪i aːsa്ʋad̪ika്kuna്n̪u sana്t̪aോʂaŋa്ŋaɭ
ina്d̪a്ɾijaɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪uɭa്ɭa uraʋakaɭ ʋeːɡat̪a്t̪ilaːka്kuna്n̪a ɡarbʱaːʃajaŋa്ŋaɭaːɳa്
eːt̪a് inamaːɳa് t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum d̪uɦkʰaŋa്ŋaɭ aː sana്t̪aോʂaŋa്ŋaɭ aːɾambʱika്kukajum aʋasaːnika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u
kuna്t̪ijuʈe put̪a്ɾaː bud̪a്ɖʱimaːnaːja manasa്sina് aːnan̪a്d̪amila്la
at̪a്t̪aɾam kaːɾa്jaŋa്ŋaɭil ena്n̪aːl oɾu manuʂa്jan paʈʰit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaːl
aʋan ɟiːʋika്kuma്paോɻum ʃaɾiːɾat̪a്t̪inṯe t͡ʃaŋa്ŋala ʋaɦika്kuma്paോɻum
kaːmaʋum kaോpaʋum kai̯kaːɾa്jam t͡ʃeja്jaːn aʋan bʱaːɡa്jaʋaːnaːɳa്
aʋanaːɳa് juka്t̪a aʋana് sana്t̪aോʂamuɳa്ʈa്
samt̪rɨpa്t̪i ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam uɭa്ɭil aʋanṯe ɟiːʋit̪am lajit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋinṯe ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪il aʋan n̪irʋaːɳa sa്parʃika്kuna്n̪u
aŋa്ŋane rɨʂimaːr ʋiʃa്ɾamika്kuʋaːn paോkuna്n̪u
paːpaŋa്ŋaɭ ila്laːt̪aːka്ki aʋasaːnam samʃajaŋa്ŋaɭumaːji ɦrɨd̪ajaŋa്ŋaɭumaːji
bʱaɾaɳaʋum ʃaːna്t̪aʋumaːɳa് aʋar ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪a ela്laː n̪ana്majilum sana്t̪aോʂika്kuna്n̪u
d̪ai̯ʋat̪a്t̪inṯe samaːɖʱaːnat̪a്t̪ina് aʈut̪a്t̪a് ɟiːʋit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪aʋaɾela്laːm
at̪a്jaːɡa്ɾaɦat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪um ka്ɾaോɖʱat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪um oɻiʋaːji d̪iʋasaŋa്ŋaɭ kaʈana്n̪upaോkuna്n̪aʋar
aːt̪a്maːʋinejum ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭejum kiːɻaʈaka്ki aːt̪a്maːʋine arijuna്n̪u
t̪anṯe ʃaːna്t̪amaːja aːt̪a്maːʋina് purat̪a്t̪a് aʈat͡ʃa്t͡ʃiʈuna്n̪a ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱan
ina്d̪a്ɾijat̪a്t̪inṯe ela്laː sa്parʃanaʋum oɾu bana്ɖʱaʋum kaʈana്n̪upaോkaːn anuʋad̪ika്kuna്n̪ila്la
aːɾuʈe ʃaːna്t̪amaːja kaɳa്ɳukaɭ sa്t̪ʰiɾamaːja puɾikaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് n̪eːɾiʈa്ʈa് n̪aോka്kuna്n̪u
aːɾuʈe baːɦa്ja ʃa്ʋaːsaʋum akat̪a്t̪e ʃa്ʋaːsaʋum ʋalit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeʈuka്kapa്peʈuna്n̪u
n̪aːsaːɾana്ɖʱa്ɾaŋa്ŋaɭiluːʈe t̪ula്jaʋum saːʋaɖʱaːnaʋum n̪iʃa്t͡ʃalaʋum aʈut̪a്t̪um
aʋajaʋaŋa്ŋaɭ ɦrɨd̪ajam manasa്sa് ena്n̪iʋa paɾimit̪apa്peʈut̪a്t̪ijiɾika്kuna്n̪a
ʋiʈa്ʈajat͡ʃa്t͡ʃukaൊɳa്ʈa് ʋiʈut̪al laka്ʂa്jamaːka്ki
abʱiniʋeːʃam bʱajam ka്ɾaോɖʱamipa്paോɻum uɳa്ʈa്
ʋiʈut̪al labʱit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ena്n̪ena്n̪eːka്kum maോt͡ʃipa്pika്kapa്peʈa്ʈu
at̪e ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱika്kuna്n̪aʋan aːɾaːɳena്n̪a് aʋan ena്n̪e arijuna്n̪uʋala്laോ
jaːɡaʋum aːɾaːɖʱanajum d̪ai̯ʋam ʋeɭipa്peʈut̪a്t̪i
ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱika്kaːt̪a്t̪aʋan laോkaɾaka്ʂit̪aːʋaːjiɾika്kuna്n̪u
ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪a ela്laːṯṯinejum sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a d̪ai̯ʋam ʋeɭipa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːt̪a്t̪a
at̪il aːɾu ɟaːma്jaʋum paɾit͡ʃajum kaɳa്ʈet̪a്t̪um
bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪ajuʈe aɲa്t͡ʃaːm ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam iʋiʈe aʋasaːnika്kuna്n̪u
karma്masana്n̪a്jaːsajaോɡa് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭuʈe pʰalam upeːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃukaൊɳa്ʈa് mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam 
krɨʂa്ɳan
aːkajaːl jaോɡa്jamaːja pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪i t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪aʋan
ɟaോlijil n̪ina്n̪a് laːbʱam t̪eːʈuna്n̪ila്la aː manuʂa്jan ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
sana്jaːsijum jaോɡijum  ɾaɳa്ʈum ona്n̪aːɳaോ
aʋan ɟa്ʋaːla kat̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋanaോ ala്la
t̪a്jaːɡat̪a്t̪inṯe ala്leŋa്kil t͡ʃumat̪alajileːka്ka് kai̯ ʋaja്ka്kuna്n̪ila്la
uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪aʋane jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa n̪iɾaːkaɾanaːji kaɳaka്kaːka്kuka
t̪a്jaɟika്kaːt̪a്t̪aʋarka്kuʋeːɳa്ʈi ɟaോlijaːl aːɾaːɖʱika്kuka
jaോɡinaːji pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪ila്la aŋa്ŋane paraɲa്ɲat̪a് n̪ana്n̪aːji
pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭaːl ʋaോʈa്ʈar ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് ujaɾuna്n̪u

ɦrɨd̪ajam urapa്pika്kukajum ena്n̪eka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juka ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuka kaൊɳa്ʈuʋaɾika
enika്kuɭa്ɭa ʋaɻipaːʈukaɭ ena്n̪e pa്ɾaɳaːmam aːka്kuka uɳa്ʈaːka്kuka

n̪iɡuːɖʱat̪a




ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam 
krɨʂa്ɳa#
inijum d̪uːɾe keːɭka്keːɳameː n̪iːɳa്ʈa aːjuɖʱaɖʱaːɾijaːja kart̪a്t̪aːʋeː iː eːṯṯaʋum put̪ija ʋaːka്kukaɭ ɲaːn parajuna്n̪u
ena്n̪e epa്paോɻum sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a n̪inaka്ku sana്t̪aോʂaʋum samaːɖʱaːnaʋum n̪alkuʋaːn paraɲa്ɲiɾika്kuna്n̪u
maɦat̪a്t̪aːja d̪eːʋaɡaɳamaോ ɾaːɟakiːja rɨʂimaːɾaോ arijuna്n̪ila്la
paɳa്ʈeː d̪eːʋana്maːɾejum rɨʂimaːɾejum uɳa്ʈaːka്kija enṯe pa്ɾakrɨt̪i
aʋan maːt̪a്ɾameː arijuː  aʋan paːpaʋimuka്t̪anum ɟa്ɲaːnijumaːɳa്
laോkaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe n̪aːt̪ʰanaːja ena്n̪e ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃamuɭa്ɭa kaɳa്ɳukaɭaːl kaːɳuna്n̪aʋan
ɟanika്kaːt̪a്t̪a maɾika്kaːt̪a്t̪a aːɾambʱika്kaːt̪a്t̪a pa്ɾakrɨt̪ikaɭ ena്t̪aːjaːlum
ʋit̪aɾaɳam t͡ʃeja്japa്peʈuna്n̪a mart̪a്jaɾaːja manuʂa്jarka്ka് aː sa്ʋabʱaːʋaŋa്ŋaɭ ena്n̪il n̪ina്n̪aːɳa്
bud̪a്ɖʱi ʋai̯d̪aɡa്d̪a്ɖʱa്jam pa്ɾabud̪a്ɖʱat̪a saɦiʂa്ɳut̪a aːt̪a്manijana്t̪a്ɾaɳam
sat̪a്jasana്ɖʱat̪a samat̪a്ʋam d̪uɦkʰam ala്leŋa്kil aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe sana്t̪aോʂam
ɟanan̪aʋum maɾaɳaʋum bʱajaʋum n̪irbʱajaʋum laɟa്ɟajum
opa്pam baɦumaːnaʋum maɖʱuɾamuɭa്ɭa n̪iɾupad̪a്ɾaʋaʋum# samaːɖʱaːnaʋum
at̪eː
ena്t̪a് sambʱaʋika്kum sana്t̪aോʂaʋum kaɳa്ɳiːɾum bʱaka്t̪ijum mit̪aʋa്jajaʋum
n̪alkaːn aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kukajum saɦaːjika്kaːn aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪uela്laːm enṯe sama്maːnat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪aːɳa്
eːɻa് pa്ɾaɖʱaːna sana്jaːsimaːr muːpa്pana്maːr n̪aːla് kart̪a്t̪aːʋaːja manusa് seṯṯa്
enṯe ɟaോli paŋa്kiʈuna്n̪u  laോkaŋa്ŋaɭe bʱaɾika്kaːn iʋajum ɲaːn ɟanipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
pina്n̪e rɨʂikaɭum pit̪rɨkaɭum manukaɭum ela്laːʋaɾum enṯe manasa്sinṯe oɾu t͡ʃina്t̪ajaːl
iː laോkat̪a്t̪e n̪iraja്ka്kaːn manuʂa്jaʋarɡat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋamʃaŋa്ŋaɭ aʋiʈe n̪ina്n̪a് ujarn̪a്n̪u

sat̪a്jaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe aː sat̪a്jaminimut̪al ena്n̪aോʈuɭa്ɭa kuṯṯamaṯṯa ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪il bana്ɖʱapa്peʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪u
at̪e ela്laːṯṯinṯejum uraʋiʈam ena്n̪e arijuna്n̪u ela്laː srɨʂa്ʈikaɭum ɲaːn srɨʂa്ʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
aːt̪a്maːʋiluɭa്ɭa ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭ ena്n̪aോʈu paṯṯit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːrn̪a്n̪u enṯe sat̪a്t̪ajileːka്ka് kaൊɳa്ʈuʋana്n̪u
ɦrɨd̪ajaŋa്ŋaɭ ena്n̪il urapa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu n̪iʃa്ʋaːsaŋa്ŋaɭ ena്n̪ileːka്ka് n̪iʃa്ʋasit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ena്n̪e sa്t̪ut̪ika്kuna്n̪u oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪aɾum
at̪inaːl aʋarka്ka് sana്t̪aോʂaʋum samaːɖʱaːnaʋum uɳa്ʈa് bʱaka്t̪ijuɭa്ɭa t͡ʃina്t̪ajum samsaːɾaʋum
iʋaɾaോʈa്  aŋa്ŋane n̪ana്n̪aːji seːʋika്kuna്n̪u aŋa്ŋane n̪irt̪a്t̪aːt̪e sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪u

ela്laːʋaɾum aʋaɾaോʈuɭa്ɭa sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inaːji aʋaɾuʈe iɾuɳa്ʈa aːt̪a്maːʋil ɲaːn ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
kuːʈaːt̪e ɟa്ɲaːnad̪iːpat̪a്t̪inṯe ʃaോbʱajuɭa്ɭa kiɾaɳaŋa്ŋaɭaːl aʋaɾuʈe aɟa്ɲat̪a akaṯṯuna്n̪u

ela്laːʋaɾejum piʈikuːʈuna്n̪a kaja്peːrija maɾaɳam sana്t̪aോʂakaɾamaːja peʈa്ʈena്n̪uɭa്ɭa ɟanan̪am

ela്laːt̪a്t̪ilum ela്laːt̪a്t̪ilum n̪ina്n̪il n̪ina്n̪a് ela്laːʋaɾum ujirt̪a്t̪eɻuna്n̪eːṯṯiɾika്kuna്n̪u
ipa്paോɭ ɲaːn kaːɳuna്n̪at̪a് asamkʰa്jamaːɳa്
ʋaʃaŋa്ŋaɭ n̪inṯeːt̪aːɳa്
ʋaːju# n̪iːjaːɳa് t̪aʈaʋukaːɾan
n̪aɾakinṯe jama iɾuɳa്ʈa
opa്pam aɡa്n̪ijuʈe t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪a t̪iːpa്paൊɾijum
ʋaɾuɳanṯe t̪iɾakaɭ n̪inṯe t̪iɾamaːlakaɭaːɳa് t͡ʃana്d̪a്ɾanum n̪aka്ʂat̪a്ɾapa്ɾakaːʃaʋum
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈeːt̪aːɳa് pa്ɾaɟaːpat̪i
n̪iːjaːɳaോ at̪a് n̪inaka്kuɭa്ɭat̪aːɳa്
paɻaja laോkat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋid̪uːɾa ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്t̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪at̪il aʋar muʈa്ʈukut̪a്t̪i

ʋiːɳa്ʈum d̪ai̯ʋameː ʋiːɳa്ʈum
aːjiɾam maʈaŋa്ŋa് ʋalut̪aːka്kaʈa്ʈe
baɦumaːnaʋum aːɾaːɖʱanajum 
maɦat̪a്ʋaʋum sa്t̪ut̪ijum  n̪inaka്ku
n̪amaോ n̪amasa്t̪eː ela്laː bʱaːɡat̪a്t̪um n̪ilaʋiɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
iʋiʈe mukaɭil t̪aːɻe kaɾaɲa്ɲu
n̪iː paോkuma്paോɭ paraɲa്ɲu

n̪amaോsa്t̪u d̪ai̯ʋam aːɾaːɖʱit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
n̪amaോsa്t̪u peːɾila്laːt̪a്t̪a kart̪a്t̪aːʋeː

kaːɾaɳam n̪iːjaːɳa് ela്laːm at̪e n̪iː
aːɦa് ipa്paോɭ d̪eːʂa്jat̪a്t̪ilaːɳeŋa്kil
ɲaːn n̪ina്n̪e suɦrɨt̪a്t̪aːji kaɾut̪ijiɾuna്n̪at̪aːji n̪iː oːrka്kaɳam
laɭit̪amaːja samsaːɾat̪a്t̪il samsaːɾika്kuka
puɾuʂana്maːr oːɾaോn̪a്n̪inum oːɾaോn̪a്n̪um upajaോɡika്kuna്n̪at̪upaോle
n̪ina്n̪e krɨʂa്ɳaː ɾaːɟakumaːɾan ena്n̪a് ʋiɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaോ manasa്silaːka്kijila്la
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe maraɲa്ɲiɾika്kuna്n̪a maɦat̪a്ʋam
ʃaka്t̪i n̪inṯe bʱajam

ala്leŋa്kil ɲaŋa്ŋaɭ ʋiʃa്ɾamika്kuma്paോɭ

oṯṯaja്ka്ka് ala്leŋa്kil kuːʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪il
paɾiʃud̪a്ɖʱan n̪iː t͡ʃeja്jeːɳameː t̪eṯṯa്

baɦumaːnika്kaːnum aːɾaːɖʱika്kaːnum

oɾu makanṯe pit̪aːʋaːji

ena്n̪aോʈa് sau̯ma്jat̪ajaോʈe

pa്ɾija kart̪a്t̪aːʋeː d̪ajaniːjamaːji

peːʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaɾaɳa്ʈa iː ɦrɨd̪ajam d̪urbalamaːɳa്

krɨʂa്ɳan
at̪e n̪iː kaɳa്ʈala്laോ arɟa്ɟunaː kaːɾaɳam ɲaːn n̪ina്n̪e n̪ana്n̪aːji sa്n̪eːɦit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾuna്n̪u
misa്ṯṯika് mana്t̪a്ɾat̪a്t̪aːl ʋeɭipa്peʈut̪a്t̪ija enṯe ɾaɦasa്ja mukʰam
t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪at̪um at̪iʃajakaɾaʋum ʋiʃaːlaʋum ɡaːmbʱiːɾa്jaʋum baɦumukʰaʋum
ela്laː ʋarʂaŋa്ŋaɭilum n̪iːjala്laːt̪e maṯṯaːɾum kaːɳaːt̪a്t̪at̪a്
ena്t̪ena്n̪aːl it̪aോ jaːɡamaോ d̪aːnamaോ ʋeːd̪am kaൊɳa്ʈala്la ʋaɾuna്n̪at̪a്
n̪ana്n̪aːji t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪a pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭaോ d̪iːrɡʱaneːɾam t̪apasa്su t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪aോ pa്ɾaːrt̪a്t̪ʰanakaɭaോ paɾiɦaːsaŋa്ŋaɭaോ ala്la
saŋa്kiːrt̪a്t̪anaŋa്ŋaɭ
anaʃa്ʋaɾamaːja aːt̪a്maːʋine ʋasa്t̪a്ɾam ɖʱaɾika്kaːt̪e kaːɳaːn aː mart̪a്ja kaɳa്ɳukaɭ saɦika്kaɳam
kuɾuka്kaɭuʈe ɾaːɟakumaːɾan it̪a് n̪iŋa്ŋaɭka്kaːji maːt̪a്ɾam suːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪u aːɦa്laːd̪aʋaːnaːjiɾika്kuka
n̪inṯe kaɳa്ɳu kaɳa്ʈat̪ukaൊɳa്ʈu n̪inṯe ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪e iɭaka്kaːt̪iɾika്kaʈa്ʈe
enṯe maɦat̪a്ʋat̪a്t̪aോʈukuːʈija enṯe bʱiːkaɾat̪a ɲaːn muma്pa് uɳa്ʈaːjiɾuna്n̪at̪upaോle
aŋa്ŋane ɲaːn ʋiːɳa്ʈum n̪inaka്ku ʋeːɳa്ʈi aːjiɾika്kum iɭam ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪aോʈe it̪aː

saɲa്ɟaja

arɟa്ɟunan
ipa്paോɭ t̪iɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuʋaɾuna്n̪at̪a് kaːɳuma്paോɭ ɟanaːrd̪a്d̪ana
iː sau̯ɦrɨd̪a manuʂa്ja t͡ʃaʈa്ʈaka്kuːʈa് enṯe manasa്sina് t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kaːn kaɻijum
ʃaːna്t̪amaːja t͡ʃina്t̪akaɭ oɾika്kal kuːʈi enṯe ɦrɨd̪ajam ʋiːɳa്ʈum miʈika്kuna്n̪u
krɨʂa്ɳan
at̪e at̪a് at̪a്bʱut̪akaɾaʋum bʱajaŋa്kaɾaʋumaːjiɾuna്n̪u
pa്ɾija ɾaːɟakumaːɾane n̪iː kaɳa്ʈat̪upaോle ena്n̪e kaːɳaːn d̪ai̯ʋaŋa്ŋaɭ
n̪iɾana്t̪aɾam kaːɳaːnuɭa്ɭa bʱajaʋum aːɡa്ɾaɦaʋum
ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum ʋeːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭ kaൊɳa്ʈaോ t̪a്jaːɡam kaൊɳa്ʈaോ ala്la
t̪apasa്sumala്la sama്maːnam kaൊʈuka്kalala്la pa്ɾaːrt̪a്t̪ʰanakaൊɳa്ʈumala്la
n̪iː kaɳa്ʈat̪upaോle aːɾeŋa്kilum kaːɳumaോ

eːṯṯaʋum kiːɻaʈaŋa്ŋalum ɲaːn arijapa്peʈuna്n̪u

ela്laːt̪a്t̪ilum epa്paോɻum aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u ela്laːʋaɾejum sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪u
sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inṯe eːka laka്ʂa്jat̪a്t̪inaːji ɲaːnum ena്n̪ejum srɨʂa്ʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്

aɖʱa്jaːjam 
arɟa്ɟunan
jaɟamaːnan n̪ina്n̪e seːʋika്kuna്n̪a manuʂa്jaɾuʈeɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪il sat̪a്ja
d̪ai̯ʋam ʋeɭipa്peʈut̪a്t̪ijat̪upaോle seːʋika്kuna്n̪a puɾuʂana്maːɾuʈe
ʋeɭipa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪a ʃaɾiːɾamila്laːt̪a്t̪a d̪uːɾe n̪ina്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u
ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪inṯejum ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯejum mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa maːrɡam eːt̪aːɳa്
krɨʂa്ɳan
ena്n̪e seːʋika്kuna്n̪aʋan  ɲaːn ena്n̪et̪a്t̪ana്n̪e kaːɳika്kuna്n̪at̪upaോle 
sa്t̪ʰiɾam sat̪a്jam puːrɳa്ɳa bʱaka്t̪ijaോʈe sa്t̪ʰiɾamaːji
aʋar ena്n̪e ʋaɭaɾe ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱanaːji kaɾut̪una്n̪u ena്n̪aːl aːɾaːɳa് seːʋika്kuna്n̪at̪a് 
ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u ad̪rɨʃa്janaːjaʋan
ʋeɭipa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːt̪a്t̪a peːɾila്laːt̪a്t̪a t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kaːn kaɻijaːt̪a്t̪a
at̪a്jaɖʱikam sarʋa്ʋaʋa്jaːpi at̪a്juna്n̪at̪am urapa്pa്
ipa്ɾakaːɾam ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪aʋar aʋaɾuʈe ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭe ʋaʃiːkaɾika്kuna്n̪u
ela്laːʋaɾaോʈum oɾeː manasa്saോʈe ela്laː n̪ana്majilum sana്t̪aോʂika്kuna്n̪u
iː anuɡa്ɾaɦiːt̪a aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭ enṯe aʈuka്kal ʋaɾuna്n̪u
ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum kaʈʰinam
manasa്sine ʋaɭat͡ʃa്t͡ʃaൊʈika്kuna്n̪aʋarka്kuɭa്ɭat̪aːɳa് kaʂa്ʈapa്paːʈa്
aʋa്jaka്t̪amaːja aː kaːɻa്t͡ʃajila്laːt̪a്t̪a paːt̪ajilet̪a്t̪aːn
maːmsam ʋaɦika്kuna്n̪a manuʂa്jan ʋiɾaɭamaːjiɾika്kum
ena്n̪aːl oɾuʋan t̪anṯe ela്laː pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪iʈat̪a്t̪u t̪ana്n̪eː
enika്kuʋeːɳa്ʈi sa്ʋajam paɾit̪a്jaːɡam ena്n̪il n̪iraɲa്ɲu sa്t̪ʰiɾam
at̪a്juna്n̪at̪ane maːt̪a്ɾam seːʋika്kaːn ɾaːʋum pakalum
ena്n̪eka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് t͡ʃina്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u  ɲaːn aʋane ʋeːɡat̪a്t̪il ujart̪a്t̪um
ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe d̪uɾit̪at̪a്t̪inṯejum maɾaɳat̪a്t̪inṯejum samud̪a്ɾat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a്
aːɾuʈe aːt̪a്maːʋa് ena്n̪il muruke piʈika്kuna്n̪u n̪iː ena്n̪aോʈu paṯṯinilka്kuka
ɦrɨd̪ajaʋum manasa്sum kaൊɳa്ʈa് ena്n̪e keʈa്ʈipa്piʈika്kuka aŋa്ŋane n̪iː ʋasika്kum
t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum enṯe kuːʈe ujaɾat̪a്t̪il ena്n̪aːl n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe ʋit͡ʃaːɾamuɳa്ʈeŋa്kil
at̪a്ɾa ujaɾat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪uɭa്ɭa ɖa്ɾaോpa്pukaɭ n̪iː balaɦiːnan̪aːɳeŋa്kil saɟa്ɟiːkaɾika്kum
ʃaɾiːɾaʋum aːt̪a്maːʋum ena്n̪il n̪iɾana്t̪aɾam
n̪iɾaːʃapa്peʈaɾut̪a് enika്ka് kuraɲa്ɲa seːʋanam t̪aɾuː ana്ʋeːʂika്kuka
d̪rɨɖʱamaːja it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰaːʃaka്t̪ijaോʈe aːɾaːɖʱit͡ʃa്t͡ʃukaൊɳa്ʈa് ena്n̪ilet̪a്t̪aːn
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭka്ka് sa്t̪ʰiɾamaːji aːɾaːɖʱika്kaːn kaɻijuna്n̪ila്leŋa്kil
enika്kuʋeːɳa്ʈi pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuʋin enika്ku pa്ɾasaːd̪amuɭa്ɭa pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭil ad̪a്ɖʱa്ʋaːnika്kuʋin
ena്t̪ena്n̪aːl ena്n̪e sa്‌n̪eːɦika്kaːn ʋeːɳa്ʈi ad̪a്ɖʱa്ʋaːnika്kuna്n̪aʋan
oʈuʋil n̪eːʈum paka്ʂeː it̪ilaːɳeŋa്kil
n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe maŋa്ŋija ɦrɨd̪ajam paɾaːɟajapa്peʈuna്n̪u n̪iŋa്ŋaɭuʈe paɾaːɟajam enika്ka് kaൊɳa്ʈuʋaɾika kaɳa്ʈet̪a്t̪uka
ena്n̪il abʱajam aɖʱa്ʋaːnat̪a്t̪inṯe pʰalam paോkaʈa്ʈe
enika്kuʋeːɳa്ʈijuɭa്ɭa pa്ɾat̪a്jaːʃa upeːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u eɭija ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪aോʈe
aːkajaːl n̪iː ʋaɾeːɳam ena്t̪ena്n̪aːl arijaːn kuːʈut̪al uɳa്ʈeŋa്kilum
ut̪a്saːɦat̪a്t̪eːka്kaːɭ aːɾaːɖʱanajaːɳa് n̪ala്lat̪a്
arijuna്n̪at̪ineːka്kaːɭ t̪a്jaɟika്kuna്n̪at̪ineːka്kaːɭ n̪ala്lat̪a്
t̪a്jaːɡat̪a്t̪ina് aʈut̪a്t̪a്  ʋaɭaɾe aʈut̪a്t̪a് 
n̪it̪a്jaʃaːna്t̪i ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
ona്n̪um ʋeruka്kaːt̪a്t̪aʋan
ela്laː ɟiːʋaɟaːlaŋa്ŋaɭilum sa്ʋajam sau̯ma്janaːji ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u
anukama്pajuɭa്ɭa aɦaŋa്kaːɾat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് oɻiʋaːka്kapa്peʈa്ʈa
sa്ʋajam sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪at̪il n̪ina്n̪a് oɻiʋaːka്kijiɾika്kuna്n̪u maːṯṯamila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪a്
n̪ala്lat̪aോ t͡ʃiːt̪a്t̪ajaോ ka്ʂama samt̪rɨpa്t̪i urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa
ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪il sa്ʋajam pa്ɾaːʋiːɳa്jam n̪eːʈuka aʋanṯe ʋaːka്ka് paːlika്kuka
ena്n̪e ana്ʋeːʂika്kuna്n̪u ɦrɨd̪ajaʋum aːt̪a്maːʋum ena്n̪aോʈa് pa്ɾat̪iɟa്ɲa t͡ʃeja്t̪u
ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a aː manuʂa്jan t̪anṯe ʋarɡa്ɡat̪a്t̪e bud̪a്ɖʱimuʈa്ʈika്kaːt̪a്t̪aʋan
aʋaɾaːl ʋiʂamika്kuna്n̪ila്la kaോpat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് ʋa്jaka്t̪am
sana്t̪aോʂat̪a്t̪inaോ saŋa്kaʈat̪a്t̪inaോ bʱajat̪a്t̪inaോ ʋeːɳa്ʈi ʋaɭaɾe ujaɾat̪a്t̪il ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u
ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a aː manuʂa്jan aːr ʃaːna്t̪amaːja kaɳa്ɳuɭa്ɭa#
t̪uɾuma്pika്kaːt̪a്t̪a ʃaːna്t̪amaːja n̪ala്la samat̪ulit̪amaːja aːʃajaka്kuɻapa്pamila്laːt̪a്t̪a
ena്n̪aോʈaൊpa്pam pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum ela്laː pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭil n̪ina്n̪um ʋeːrpeʈa്ʈu
ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a aː manuʂa്jan ena്n̪il ʋiʃa്ʋaːsamarpa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaʋan
aːɾaോʈum paɾibʱaʋamila്la aːɾejum put͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰika്kuna്n̪ila്la sana്t̪aോʂika്kuna്n̪ila്la
n̪ana്majaോ t̪ina്majaോ sambʱaʋika്kaːn anuʋad̪ika്kaːt̪e d̪uɦkʰika്kuna്n̪ila്la
at̪a് aːʋaʃa്jamuɭa്ɭapa്paോɭ ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam at̪a് epa്paോɭ purapa്peʈum
ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a aː manuʂa്jan aːɾaːɳa് suɦrɨt̪a്t̪inum ʃat̪a്ɾuʋinum
t̪ula്ja manasa്saോʈe t̪ula്ja ɦrɨd̪ajam n̪ilanirt̪a്t̪uka
laɟa്ɟajum maɦat̪a്ʋaʋum ʋaɦika്kuna്n̪u t̪ula്ja samaːɖʱaːnat̪a്t̪aോʈe
t͡ʃuːʈum t̪aɳupa്pum sukʰaʋum ʋeːd̪anajum eʈuka്kuna്n̪u n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪u
aːɡa്ɾaɦaŋa്ŋaɭ upeːka്ʂika്kuka sa്t̪ut̪ijaോ apaʋaːd̪amaോ keːɭka്kuna്n̪u
ʋikaːɾaɾaɦit̪amaːja samjamanat̪a്t̪il oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪aɾum t͡ʃalika്kaːt̪e
bʱuːmijumaːji bana്ɖʱamila്laːt̪a്t̪a ena്n̪il urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃunilka്kuna്n̪a
ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪a aː manuʂa്jan ena്n̪aːl ela്laːṯṯinumupaɾijaːji ɲaːn sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪u
ɟiːʋika്kaːnuɭa്ɭa ɟiːʋit̪am aːrka്kaːɳaോ aː sana്t̪uʂa്ʈar
t̪iːka്ʂa്ɳamaːja ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪ilum kaːɳaːt̪a്t̪a sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪ilum
enṯe ɟiːʋanṯe anuɡa്ɾaɦiːt̪amaːja amrɨt̪a് kuʈika്kuna്n̪u
iʋiʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam  bʱaɡaʋad̪a് ɡiːt̪ajuʈe
bʱaka്t̪ijaോɡa് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪inṯe mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam 
arɟa്ɟunan
krɨpajuɭa്ɭa keːʃaʋaː ipa്paോɭ ɲaːn keːɭka്kum#
t̪aോn̪a്n̪una്n̪a ɟiːʋanṯejum at̪inapa്puramuɭa്ɭa aːt̪a്maːʋinṯejum
n̪amuka്ka് ena്t̪aːɳa് arijaːʋuna്n̪at̪a്ala്leŋa്kil arijaɳamena്n̪a് kaɾut̪una്n̪u
krɨʂa്ɳan
at̪e kuna്t̪ijuʈe put̪a്ɾan iː maːmsam n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ kaːɳuna്n̪u
ka്ʂeːt̪a്ɾam ɟiːʋan t̪uɭuma്puna്n̪a meːkʰalajaːɳa്
at̪a് kaːɳukajum arijukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪a് aːt̪a്maːʋaːɳa്
ka്ʂeːt̪a്ɾaɟa്ɲa ela്laː ʋajalukaɭilum ina്t̪a്jan ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
ɲaːn ka്ʂeːt̪a്ɾaɟa്ɲanaːɳa് ɲaːn ena്t̪aːɳa് sarʋeːkaɭ
aː ariʋina് maːt̪a്ɾameː arijuː arijaːʋuna്n̪aʋaje arijuː
arijuna്n̪aʋan mukʰeːna# at̪ena്t̪aːɳa് ɟiːʋanṯe aː maɳa്ɖalam
it̪ina് ena്t̪a് ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭuɳa്ʈa് at̪a് eʋiʈe n̪ina്n̪aːɳa്
ena്t̪ukaൊɳa്ʈaːɳa് it̪a് maːruna്n̪at̪a് faːka്kalṯṯijum
at̪a് ʋisa്majipa്pika്kuna്n̪u it̪inṯe ʃaka്t̪i
ena്n̪il n̪ina്n̪a് it̪a് eŋa്ŋane keːɭka്kuna്n̪u

ɡʱaʈakaŋa്ŋaɭ baോɖʱapuːrʋamaːja ɟiːʋit̪am manasa്sa്
ad̪rɨʃa്jamaːja supa്ɾaɖʱaːna ʃaka്t̪i oma്pat̪a് ʋit͡ʃit̪a്ɾa kaʋaːʈaŋa്ŋaɭ
ʃaɾiːɾat̪a്t̪inṯe ina്d̪a്ɾijat̪a്t̪inṯe aɲa്t͡ʃa് meːkʰalakaɭ
aːɡa്ɾaɦam aniʂa്ʈam sukʰaʋum ʋeːd̪anajum t͡ʃina്t̪ajum
aːɻat̪a്t̪il n̪eja്t̪at̪um n̪ilanilka്kaːnuɭa്ɭa sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪ajum
iʋajela്laːm aːt̪a്maːʋinaːl srɨʂa്ʈika്kapa്peʈa്ʈaʋajaːɳa്
ʋinajam sat̪a്jasana്ɖʱat̪a n̪iɾupad̪a്ɾaʋat̪a്ʋam
ka്ʂamajum baɦumaːnaʋum ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭaോʈuɭa്ɭa baɦumaːnaʋum
ʃud̪a്ɖʱi sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪a sa്ʋajam n̪ijana്t̪a്ɾaɳam
ina്d̪a്ɾijasukʰaŋa്ŋaɭe n̪ina്d̪ika്kuka aːt̪a്mat̪a്jaːɡam
ɾaോɡijuʈe urapa്pineka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuɭa്ɭa ɖʱaːɾaɳa
ɟanan̪am maɾaɳam pa്ɾaːjam ɾaോɡam kaʂa്ʈapa്paːʈukaɭ paːpam ena്n̪iʋajil
ɖiṯṯaːt͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്‌menṯa് ʋiːʈa്ʈileːka്ka് laɡʱuʋaːji piʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്
maka്kaɭum bʱaːɾa്jajum puɾuʂana്maːɾe bana്ɖʱika്kuna്n̪at̪ela്laːm
bʱaːɡa്jat̪a്t̪il epa്paോɻum ʃaːna്t̪amaːja ɦrɨd̪ajam
t̪ina്majuʈe bʱaːɡa്jam urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰaːʃaka്t̪ijaോʈe
ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kaːn  ena്n̪e maːt̪a്ɾam n̪irt̪a്t̪una്n̪ila്la
ela്laː eːkaːna്t̪at̪akaɭejum sa്n̪eːɦika്kuna്n̪u ʃaba്d̪aŋa്ŋaɭ oɻiʋaːka്kuna്n̪u
ʋiɖa്ɖʱikaɭaːja ɟanaka്kuːʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪inṯe d̪rɨɖʱaniʃa്t͡ʃajat̪a്t̪aോʈejuɭa്ɭa ʃa്ɾamaŋa്ŋaɭ
paɾamaːt̪a്maːʋineka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃuɭa്ɭa ɖʱaːɾaɳajilet̪a്t̪aːn
at̪a് ena്t̪a് n̪eːʈa്ʈamaːɳena്n̪a് manasa്silaːka്kaːnuɭa്ɭa krɨpajum
at̪inaːl n̪eːʈijeʈuka്kaːn  it̪aːɳa് jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa ɟa്ɲaːnam ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
ala്laːt̪a്t̪at̪a് aɟa്ɲat̪ajaːɳa്
ipa്paോɭ ɲaːn arijaːn eːṯṯaʋum mikat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa ariʋineka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് samsaːɾika്kum
manuʂa്jana് amrɨt̪a് kuʈika്kaːn n̪alkuna്n̪a sat̪a്jam
aʋanṯe sat̪a്jam paɾaba്ɾaɦa്mam ela്laːm
srɨʂa്ʈika്kapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪at̪a് asat̪a്t̪a് ala്la sat̪a് ala്la
ɾuːpamaോ ɾuːpapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪at̪aോ ala്la ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum ɾaɳa്ʈum at̪ilaɖʱikaʋum
aːɾuʈe kai̯kaɭaːɳa് ela്laːjiʈat̪a്t̪um ela്laːjiʈat̪a്t̪um
aʋanṯe paːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭum ela്laːjiʈat̪a്t̪um aʋanṯe kaɳa്ɳukaɭum n̪aʈa്ʈu
n̪aോka്kuna്n̪u ela്laːjiʈat̪a്t̪um aʋanṯe t͡ʃeʋi
keːɭka്kuna്n̪u ela്laːjiʈat̪a്t̪um aʋanṯe ela്laː mukʰaŋa്ŋaɭum
aʋanṯe laോkaŋa്ŋaɭe pa്ɾakaːʃipa്pika്kuna്n̪at̪um ʋalajam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪um
aʋan n̪alkija ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭil maɦat̪a്ʋapa്peʈut̪a്t̪i
eŋa്kilum aʋan baോɖʱat̪a്t̪ina് at̪iːt̪anaːɳa് ela്laːm n̪ilanirt̪a്t̪una്n̪u
ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum aʋan bana്ɖʱamila്laːt̪e ʋasika്kuna്n̪u ɾuːpaŋa്ŋaɭuʈejum ɾiːt̪ikaɭuʈejum
ɡuɾu ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum aʋana് ɾuːpamaോ ɾiːt̪ijaോ ila്la
aʋan ela്laː ɟiːʋikaɭka്kum uɭa്ɭiluɳa്ʈa്  kuːʈaːt̪e 
anaŋa്ŋaːt̪e ipa്paോɻum t͡ʃalika്kuna്n̪u ʋiʋeːt͡ʃit͡ʃa്t͡ʃila്la
t̪alka്ʂaɳa saːna്n̪iɖʱa്jat̪a്t̪inṯe suːka്ʂa്mat̪aja്ka്kaːji aʈut̪a്t̪a്
ela്laːʋarka്kum oːɾaോɾut̪a്t̪arka്kum ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum aɭaʋila്laːt̪e d̪uːɾe
baɦumukʰamala്la ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum ipa്paോɻum n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪u
ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪a ela്laːṯṯilum ena്n̪eːka്kum arijapa്peʈaːn
samɾaka്ʂakanen̪a്n̪a n̪ilajil kaːlat̪a്t̪inṯe aʋasaːnat̪a്t̪il
aʋan ela്laːm aʋasaːnipa്pika്kukajum ʋiːɳa്ʈum srɨʂa്ʈika്kukajum t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u
ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam aʋan iɾuʈa്ʈinṯe ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪ilaːɳa്
ʃaːʃa്ʋat̪amaːji t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪u ɟa്ɲaːnam aʋanaːɳa്
ɟa്ɲaːnat̪a്t̪inṯe ʋaɻijum ela്laː ɟa്ɲaːnikaɭuʈejum ʋaɻikaːʈa്ʈijum
ela്laː ɦrɨd̪ajaŋa്ŋaɭilum n̪aʈa്ʈupiʈipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
aŋa്ŋane ɲaːn paraɲa്ɲiʈa്ʈuɳa്ʈa്
ɟiːʋit̪a saːmaɡa്ɾikaɭ ʋaːrt̪a്t̪eʈuka്kal ai̯t̪iɦa്jaŋa്ŋaɭ
manasa്silaːka്kaːn aːr ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u
it̪a് manasa്silaːka്kuna്n̪u t̪iːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaːjum enṯe aʈuka്kal ʋaɾum
pa്ɾakrɨt̪ijum aːt̪a്maːʋum ɾaɳa്ʈum uɳa്ʈena്n̪a് n̪iː arijuka
t̪uʈaka്kamila്la aː ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭ arijuka
aʋajil maːṯṯam ʋaɾut̪a്t̪una്n̪at̪a് pa്ɾakrɨt̪ijaːɳa്

paോjaʋane arijaːnuɭa്ɭa aʈajaːɭaŋa്ŋaɭaːɳiʋa
muːna്n̪a് maോɖukaɭ kaɻiɲa്ɲaോ aʋan eŋa്ŋane ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪u ena്t̪a് ʋaɻi
t̪a്ɾiːfaോɭɖa് maോɖukaɭka്kapa്puram aʋane suɾaka്ʂit̪amaːji n̪ajika്kumaോ
krɨʂa്ɳan
samat͡ʃit̪a്t̪at̪ajaോʈe sarʋeː n̪aʈat̪a്t̪una്n̪aʋan
n̪ana്majuʈe t̪iɭaka്kam abʱiniʋeːʃat̪a്t̪inṯe kalaɦam alasat̪a
ariʋila്laːja്ma kaൊɳa്ʈa് aʋaɾaːɳeŋa്kil d̪eːʂa്japa്peʈila്la
aʋar ala്laːt̪a്t̪apa്paോɭ aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kila്la iɾika്kuna്n̪aʋan
aʋaɾuʈe iʈajil oɾu ʋid̪eːʃijum apaɾit͡ʃit̪anum
asa്ʋasa്t̪ʰat̪ajaോʈe n̪ina്n̪ukaൊɳa്ʈa് paraɲa്ɲuʃaːna്t̪am
pa്ɾaʃa്‌n̪aŋa്ŋaɭ paൊʈa്ʈipa്purapa്peʈuma്paോɭ iʋajaːɳa് ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭ
aʋan  sa്ʋajam keːna്d̪a്ɾiːkrɨt̪a  d̪uɦkʰaʋum sana്t̪aോʂaʋum
oɾu ʋaːka്ka് paോle ʃaba്d̪am aːɻat̪a്t̪il kaːɳuna്n̪a kaɳa്ɳukaɭileːka്ka്
kaʈa്ʈajum maːrbiɭum sa്ʋarɳa്ɳaʋum ona്n̪aːɳa്
aːɾuʈe t̪ula്ja ɦrɨd̪ajam at̪eː sau̯ma്jat̪a pulart̪a്t̪una്n̪u
manaോɦaɾaʋum iʂa്ʈapa്peʈaːt̪a്t̪at̪umaːja kaːɾa്jaŋa്ŋaɭka്kaːji urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃunilka്kuka
pa്ɾaʃamsajilum apakiːrt̪a്t̪ijilum sana്t̪uʂa്ʈan t̪rɨpa്t̪ijaːji
baɦumaːnat̪a്t̪aോʈejaോ apamaːnat̪a്t̪aോʈejaോ suɦrɨt̪a്t̪uka്kaɭka്ka്
saɦiʂa്ɳut̪ajil oɾupaോle ʃat̪a്ɾuka്kaɭaോʈum
ud̪a്jamaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋeːrpeʈa്ʈuaʋan n̪aːmakaɾaɳam t͡ʃeja്japa്peʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪u
ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭe marikaʈaka്kuna്n̪aʋan
kuːʈaːt̪e aŋa്ŋane
eːkamaːja t̪iːka്ʂa്ɳamaːja ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪aോʈe ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u
ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭka്kapa്puram kaʈana്n̪upaോkuna്n̪u anuɾuːpamaːka്kuna്n̪u
ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋinaോʈa് ena്n̪e pa്ɾaːpika്kuna്n̪u
kaːɾaɳam ɲaːnaːɳa്
ba്ɾaɦa്maːʋinṯe saːd̪rɨʃa്jam enṯeːt̪a്
amrɨt̪a് aːɳa് anaʃa്ʋaɾat̪ajum
enṯet̪aːɳa് opa്pam enṯe perfeka്ṯṯa് felisiṯṯi
iʋiʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam  aʋasaːnika്kuna്n̪u bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪ajuʈe
ɡuɳat̪a്ɾajaʋibʱaːɡajaോɡa് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋeːrpeʈut̪a്t̪i mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam 
krɨʂa്ɳan
puɾuʂana്maːr aʃa്ʋat̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪e ʋiɭika്kuna്n̪u aːlmaɾam
at̪ina് t̪aːɻe kaൊma്pukaɭum mukaɭil ʋeːɾukaɭumuɳa്ʈa് 
ena്n̪um ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱamaːja ʋrɨka്ʂam at̪e at̪inṯe ilakaɭka്kaːji
sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪e mana്t̪a്ɾika്kuna്n̪a pat͡ʃa്t͡ʃajum alajaʈika്kuna്n̪at̪umaːja sa്t̪ut̪ikaɭaːɳaോ
aʃa്ʋat̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪e arijuna്n̪aʋan ʋeːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭe ela്laːm arijuna്n̪aʋan
at̪inṯe ʃikʰaɾaŋa്ŋaɭ aːkaːʃat̪a്t̪eːka്kum bʱuːmijileːka്kum t̪aːɻuna്n̪u#
aʋaɾuʈe ɟana്mam eʈuka്kuna്n̪a manuʂa്jaɾuʈe pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ paോle t̪ana്n̪e
ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪a് at̪inṯe ʋeɭa്ɭi sa്pa്ɾeːkaɭum puːka്kaɭum
at̪inṯe t͡ʃuṯṯaɭaʋinṯe ela്laː aːkaːmka്ʂajuɭa്ɭa pat͡ʃa്t͡ʃapa്pum
suːɾa്janṯejum ʋaːjuʋinṯejum t͡ʃumbanat̪a്t̪il peʈa്ʈena്n̪uɭa്ɭa ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് kut̪ika്kuka
puɾuʂana്maːɾuʈe ɟiːʋit̪am pa്ɾalaോbʱanaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe meːɭajileːka്ka് ʋeːɡat̪a്t̪ilaːka്kuma്paോɭ
ʋuːjimɡa് sensa് at̪inṯe t̪uːŋa്ŋika്kiʈaka്kuna്n̪a ruːʈa്ʈa്‌leṯṯukaɭ ana്ʋeːʂika്kuna്n̪u
t̪aːɻe maɳa്ɳa് at̪a് aʋiʈe piʈika്kaːn saɦaːjika്kuna്n̪u
manuʂa്jaɾuʈe iː laോkat̪a്t̪iniʈajil n̪aʈaka്kuna്n̪a pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ paോle
epa്paോɻumuɭa്ɭa murukuna്n̪a bana്ɖʱanaŋa്ŋaɭiluːʈe aʋaje ʋiːɳa്ʈum bana്ɖʱipa്pika്kuka
ʋrɨka്ʂat̪a്t̪inṯe upad̪eːʃam n̪iŋa്ŋaɭka്ka് n̪ana്n̪aːji arijaːmeŋa്kil
at̪inṯe aːkrɨt̪i ena്t̪aːɳa് parajuna്n̪at̪a് at̪a് eʋiʈe n̪ina്n̪a് uraʋeʈuka്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪iʈa്ʈa്
at̪a് eŋa്ŋane aʋasaːnika്kaɳam at̪inṯe ela്laː d̪aോʂaŋa്ŋaɭum
muːrt͡ʃa്t͡ʃajuɭa്ɭa ɖiṯṯaːt͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്‌menṯinṯe kaോʈaːli n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ uɳart̪a്t̪um
paṯṯipa്piʈit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪a paːma്pa് ʋeːɾukaɭ piɭarn̪a്n̪a് kiʈaka്kuka
ina്d̪a്ɾijaɟiːʋan t̪aːɻa്n̪a്n̪a iː aʃa്ʋat̪a്t̪ʰamaʈaja്ka്kaːn
sana്t̪aോʂakaɾamaːja aː aːkaːʃat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് put̪ija ʋaɭart͡ʃa്t͡ʃakaɭ ujarn̪a്n̪uʋaɾuna്n̪u
at̪il et̪a്t̪una്n̪aʋarka്ka് maɾika്kaːn d̪iʋasamila്la
maːɲa്ɲupaോkaɾut̪a് ʋiːɻaɾut̪a്  aʋanileːka്ka് ɲaːn art̪a്t̪ʰamaːka്kuna്n̪at̪a്
pit̪aːʋum ona്n̪aːmanum aːɾaːɳa് ɾaɦasa്jam uɳa്ʈaːka്kijat̪a്
paɻaja srɨʂa്ʈijuʈe aʋar aʋanṯe aʈuka്kaleːka്ku ʋaɾuna്n̪u
abʱiniʋeːʃat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪um paൊʈa്ʈipa്paോkuna്n̪a sa്ʋapa്n̪aŋa്ŋaɭil n̪ina്n̪um
aʋaɾe maːmsat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് paɾimit̪apa്peʈut̪a്t̪una്n̪a bana്ɖʱaŋa്ŋaɭe ʋeːrpeʈut̪a്t̪una്n̪at̪a് aːɾaːɳa്
opa്pamat̪a്juna്n̪at̪anaːja aʋane epa്paോɻum aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u
eːt̪a് kaːṯṯinṯe kaːɾuɳa്jat̪a്t̪il ini ʋaɭaɾaɾut̪a്
ʋeːnalka്kaːlat̪a്t̪e aːnan̪a്d̪am uraŋa്ŋuna്n̪a maɾaŋa്ŋaɭe uɳart̪a്t̪una്n̪u
kaൊʈuŋa്kaːṯṯinṯe et̪a്ɾa sa്faോʈanam aʋaɾe kiːrimurika്kuna്n̪u kaൊma്pum t̪aɳa്ʈum
ʃaːʃa്ʋat̪amaːja laോkat̪a്t̪eːka്ka് it̪upaോluɭa്ɭa kaʈana്n̪upaോkuka
aʋiʈe maṯṯaൊɾu suːɾa്jan pa്ɾakaːʃika്kuna്n̪u maṯṯaൊɾu t͡ʃana്d̪a്ɾan
maṯṯaൊɾu ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam sana്ɖʱa്jajaോ pa്ɾabʱaːt̪amaോ ut͡ʃa്t͡ʃajaോ ala്la
oɾika്kal kaːɳuna്n̪aʋar pina്n̪e maʈaŋa്ŋiʋaɾuna്n̪ila്la
aʋar enṯe ʋiʃa്ɾamam pa്ɾaːpit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe eːṯṯaʋum ʋalija anuɡa്ɾaɦam
pa്ɾat̪a്jaka്ʂamaːja ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe iː laോkat̪a്t̪a് epa്paോɭ
maɾika്kaːt̪a്t̪a aːt̪a്maːʋa് ena്n̪il n̪ina്n̪a് purapa്peʈuna്n̪u
ɾuːpam pa്ɾaːpika്kuna്n̪u at̪a് t̪ana്n̪ileːka്ka് aːkarʂika്kuna്n̪u
biːjimɡinṯe kalaʋarajil n̪ina്n̪a് ela്laːm uɭka്kaൊɭa്ɭuna്n̪a
ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭum bud̪a്ɖʱijum paɾamaːɖʱikaːɾa aːt̪a്maːʋa്
aŋa്ŋane ɟaɖat̪a്t̪il pa്ɾaʋeːʃika്kuka ala്leŋa്kil at̪a് upeːka്ʂika്kuka
kaːṯṯa് suɡana്ɖʱam ʃeːkʰaɾika്kuna്n̪at̪upaോle iʋa ʃeːkʰaɾika്kuna്n̪u
puʂa്pa kiʈaka്kakaɭka്ka് mukaɭil ʋiːʃuna്n̪u t͡ʃeʋijum kaɳa്ɳum
sa്parʃika്kuka ɾut͡ʃika്kuka maɳaka്kuka iʋajela്laːm aːʋaʃa്jamaːɳa് 
at̪e opa്pam oɾu ʋikaːɾaːɖʱiːnamaːja manasa്sum sa്ʋajam bana്ɖʱipa്pika്kuna്n̪u
kaːɾa്jaŋa്ŋaɭ manasa്silaːka്kaːn  aŋa്ŋane
ariʋila്laːt̪a്t̪aʋar
aː aːt̪a്maːʋa് paോkuma്paോɻum ʋaɾuma്paോɻum aʈajaːɭapa്peʈut̪a്t̪aɾut̪a്
aʋan ɾuːpat̪a്t̪il t̪anṯe aːnan̪a്d̪am sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kuma്paോɭ
ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭumaːji samjaോɟipa്pit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪aːl aʋar ʋa്jaka്t̪amaːji kaːɳuna്n̪u
aːrka്kaːɳa് kaːɳaːn kaɳa്ɳuɭa്ɭat̪a് paɾiʃud̪a്ɖʱaːt̪a്maːka്kaɭ kaːɳuna്n̪u
at̪inaːji paɾiʃa്ɾamika്kuna്n̪aʋa pa്ɾabud̪a്ɖʱaɾaːja aʋar ɡa്ɾaɦika്kuna്n̪u
t̪aŋa്ŋaɭiluɭa്ɭa aː aːt̪a്maːʋa് ena്n̪aːl ʋiɖa്ɖʱikaɭ
aʋar pa്ɾajat̪a്n̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃaːlum ɦrɨd̪ajamuɭa്ɭaʋaɾaːji ʋiʋeːt͡ʃit͡ʃa്t͡ʃarijuna്n̪ila്la
d̪ajajila്laːt̪a്t̪a ʋiʋaɾamila്laːt̪a്t̪a
ena്n̪il n̪ina്n̪um arijuka
suːɾa്jana്maːɾuʈe maɦat̪a്ʋat̪a്t̪e pa്ɾakaːʃipa്pika്kuna്n̪u
at̪a് laോkat̪a്t̪e muɻuʋan pa്ɾakaːʃipa്pika്kuna്n̪u ena്n̪il n̪ina്n̪a് upaɡa്ɾaɦaŋa്ŋaɭ
ʋeɭa്ɭit̪a്t̪iɾakaɭ ʋaɾaja്ka്kuka uɡa്ɾamaːja sau̯na്d̪aɾa്jam t̪iːjiʈuka
ɲaːn kaɭimaɳa്ɳil t̪uɭat͡ʃa്t͡ʃukajaruna്n̪u ela്laː ɾuːpaŋa്ŋaɭum kaʈam kaൊʈuka്kuna്n̪u
aʋaɾuʈe ɟiːʋaʃaka്t̪i ɲaːn t͡ʃeʈijileːka്ka് t̪ena്n̪imaːri
ʋeːɾum ilajum puːʋum  ʋanapa്ɾad̪eːʃaŋa്ŋaɭe ɦaɾit̪aːbʱamaːka്kaːn
sa്pa്ɾimɡa് sa്ɾaʋam kaൊɳa്ʈa് supa്ɾaɖʱaːnamaːja uːʂa്maɭamaːji
ɲaːn sana്t̪aോʂat̪a്t̪aോʈe ʃa്ʋasika്kuna്n̪a fa്ɾejimukaɭil t̪iɭaŋa്ŋuna്n̪u kaʈana്n̪upaോkuna്n̪u
purat̪a്t̪eːka്kum uɭa്ɭileːka്kum uɭa്ɭa ʃa്ʋaːsam kaൊɳa്ʈa് bʱaka്ʂaɳam kaൊʈuka്kaːn
ela്laː maːmsaŋa്ŋaɭaːlum ʃaɾiːɾam#
iː laോkat̪a്t̪a് ʋeːɳa്ʈi
uɭa്ɭat̪a് ɾaɳa്ʈaːɳa് ʋibʱaɟika്kapa്peʈa്ʈat̪a് ona്n̪a്
aʋibʱaka്t̪a ona്n̪a് ɟiːʋika്kuna്n̪a ela്laː ʋasa്t̪uka്kaɭum
ʋibʱaɟika്kapa്peʈa്ʈaʋar aːɳaോ ʋeːriʈa്ʈa് iɾika്kuna്n̪at̪a്
d̪i aʋibʱaka്t̪a
aʋan ipa്paോɻum ujarn̪a്n̪at̪aːɳa്
at̪a്juna്n̪at̪an ela്laːm uɭka്kaൊɭa്ɭuna്n̪u aʋanṯe n̪aːmam kart̪a്t̪aːʋa്
ʃaːʃa്ʋat̪an paɾamaːɖʱikaːɾi aːd̪a്jam ela്laː laോkaŋa്ŋaɭejum n̪iraja്ka്kuna്n̪aʋan
aʋaɾe n̪ilanirt̪a്t̪una്n̪u opa്pamapa്puram ʋasika്kuna്n̪u
ʋibʱaɟit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪um aʋibʱaka്t̪aʋumɲaːn
ɲaːn manuʂa്jaɾaːlum ʋeːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭaːlum ʋiɭika്kapa്peʈuna്n̪u ɟiːʋan paɾamaോn̪a്n̪at̪amaːɳa്
puɾuʂaോt̪a്t̪aman
ena്n̪e iŋa്ŋane aːrka്karijaːm
manasa്sa് muːʈika്keʈa്ʈaːt̪e ela്laːm arijuna്n̪u pa്ɾija ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
aʋanṯe puːrɳa്ɳaːt̪a്maːʋukaൊɳa്ʈum ena്n̪e aːɾaːɖʱika്kuna്n̪u
ipa്paോɭ ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱaʋum ɾaɦasa്jaʋumaːja ɾaɦasa്jamaːɳa്
n̪ina്n̪aോʈa് pa്ɾakʰa്jaːpit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu aːɾaːɳa് it̪a് manasa്silaːka്kuna്n̪at̪a്
ɟa്ɲaːnamuɳa്ʈa് aʋan aːnan̪a്d̪at̪a്t̪il ɟaോli upeːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
iʋiʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam  aʋasaːnika്kuna്n̪u bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪ajuʈe
puɾuʂaോt̪a്t̪amapa്ɾaːpa്t̪ijaോɡa് ena്n̪a t̪alaka്keʈa്ʈil
ala്leŋa്kil paɾamaോn̪a്n̪at̪a pa്ɾaːpit͡ʃa്t͡ʃukaൊɳa്ʈa് mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe pusa്t̪akam




aɖʱa്jaːjam 
krɨʂa്ɳan
n̪irbʱajam aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe eːkat̪a്ʋam it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰa
ɟa്ɲaːnat̪a്t̪inaːji epa്paോɻum paɾiʃa്ɾamika്kuka kai̯ t̪urana്n̪u
opa്pam ʋiʃapa്pine n̪ijana്t̪a്ɾika്kuna്n̪u bʱaka്t̪ijum
opa്pam eːkaːna്t̪amaːja paʈʰanat̪a്t̪aോʈuɭa്ɭa iʂa്ʈaʋum ʋinajam
n̪eːɾuɭa്ɭaʋa ɟiːʋanuɭa്ɭa jaːt̪aൊn̪a്n̪inejum muriʋeːlpa്pika്kaːn ʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱika്kuka
sat̪a്jasana്ɖʱat̪a kaോpat̪a്t̪ileːka്kuɭa്ɭa mana്d̪at̪a oɾu manasa്sa്
at̪a് maṯṯuɭa്ɭaʋar ʋilamat̪ika്kuna്n̪at̪ine n̪isa്saːɾamaːji t̪aɭa്ɭika്kaɭajuna്n̪u
opa്pam samat͡ʃit̪a്t̪at̪a d̪aːnaɖʱarma്mam
aʋan aːɾuʈejum t̪eṯṯukaɭ oṯṯunaോka്kuna്n̪ila്la opa്pam aːrd̪a്ɾat̪ajum

ka്ʂamajaോʈe ɖʱai̯ɾa്jat̪a്t̪aോʈe ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱijaോʈe

oː ina്t̪a്jan ɾaːɟakumaːɾan kaːlukaɭ pat̪iɲa്ɲaʋanṯe

ʋaɲa്t͡ʃana aɦaŋa്kaːɾam aɦaŋa്kaːɾam

sa്ʋarɡa്ɡiːja ɟanan̪am maോt͡ʃanat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് kaൊɳa്ʈuʋaɾuna്n̪u
at̪inaːl n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ ariɲa്ɲiɾika്kaɳam asuɾana്maːɾaോʈaൊpa്pamuɭa്ɭa ɟanan̪am
bana്ɖʱanat̪a്t̪ileːka്ka് kaൊɳa്ʈuʋaɾuna്n̪u ɾaːɟakumaːɾaː sana്t̪aോʂaʋaːnaːjiɾika്kuka
aːɾuʈe t͡ʃiːʈa്ʈa് sa്ʋarɡiːja ɟanan̪at̪a്t̪inaːji n̪iːka്kiʋat͡ʃa്t͡ʃiɾika്kuna്n̪u

d̪ai̯ʋikaʋum d̪ai̯ʋikaʋum ɲaːn n̪ina്n̪aോʈu samsaːɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu

at̪inaːl ʋaɭaɾe ʃaka്t̪amaːja ʋiʃapa്pa് kaൊt̪it͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
maോʃamaːja bʱaka്ʂaɳaʋum uɳa്ʈa്  ɾaːt̪a്ɾijil n̪ina്n̪a് suːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u#
d̪urɡana്ɖʱamila്laːt̪a്t̪at̪um ʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikeʈa്ʈat̪um malinamaːjat̪a് bʱaka്ʂika്kum
aɻukalinṯe ʋiɾuna്n̪a് t͡ʃuɳa്ʈukaɭka്kaːji kaɳa്ʈumuʈa്ʈuka
iɾuʈa്ʈa് ena്n̪a sa്n̪eːɦam paോlejuɭa്ɭaʋajil

it̪a് ɲaːn t͡ʃeja്jaɳam
sau̯t̪a്t̪a്faːsa്ṯṯa് aːt͡ʃaːɾamaːɳa് ena്n̪aːl n̪eːʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪inuʋeːɳa്ʈi t̪a്jaːɡam t͡ʃeja്juka
n̪ala്la pa്ɾaʃasa്t̪ika്ka് ʋaːɡa്d̪aːnam t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪u it̪a് urapa്paːka്kuka
ɦeː bʱaɾat̪ana്maːɾil ʃa്ɾeːʂa്ʈʰan ɾaːɟaːt͡ʃaːɾamaːɳa്
paːʂan ena്n̪a mud̪a്ɾajaോʈe opa്pam oɾu t̪a്jaːɡaʋum
n̪ijamaŋa്ŋaɭka്ka് ʋiɾud̪a്ɖʱamaːji ʋaːɡa്‌d̪aːnam t͡ʃeja്‌t̪u ɖa്juː ɖaോɭ ila്laːt̪e
jaːt̪aൊɾu akama്paʈijum kuːʈaːt̪e bʱaka്ʂaɳam kaൊʈuka്kuna്n̪u
ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱamaːja sa്t̪ut̪iɡiːt̪amaോ puɾaോɦit̪ana്maːɾaോʈa് ʋalijat̪aോt̪il
ʋiʃa്ʋaːsamila്laːt̪a്t̪a aːɡʱaോʂat̪a്t̪il at̪ine n̪iːt͡ʃamaːji ʋiɭika്kuka
ana്ɖʱakaːɾamnaʂa്ʈapa്peʈa്ʈu
d̪ai̯ʋaːɾaːɖʱana
meriṯṯimɡa് aːɾaːɖʱana t̪aːɻa്n̪a്n̪a baɦumaːnam
ɾaɳa്ʈut̪aʋaɳa ɟanit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaʋar aɖʱa്jaːpakar mut̪irn̪a്n̪aʋar ʃud̪a്ɖʱi
krɨt̪a്janiʂa്ʈʰajum ba്ɾaɦa്mat͡ʃaːɾa്ja pa്ɾat̪iɟa്ɲajum
ala്laːt̪e n̪isa്saɦaːjamaːja oɾu kaːɾa്jat̪a്t̪inum muriʋeːlpa്pika്kaɾut̪a്
iʋa n̪ijamat̪a്t̪inṯe jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa mat̪aːt̪a്makat̪a uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪u
oɾu manuʂa്janejum kaʂa്ʈapa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːt̪a്t̪a ʋaːka്kukaɭ oɾika്kalum sat̪a്jamaːja ʋaːka്kukaɭ
sau̯ma്jaʋum ima്pamuɭa്ɭat̪umaːja ʋaːka്kukaɭum n̪iŋa്ŋaɭ parajuna്n̪aʋajum
oɾu ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱa ɡa്ɾana്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪inṯe pirupirupa്pa് ʋaːjanajil
iʋa samsaːɾat̪a്t̪inṯe jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa mat̪aːt̪a്makat̪a uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪u
aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe ʃaːna്t̪at̪a sau̯ma്jat̪a

pa്ɾakrɨt̪ije ʋiʃud̪a്ɖʱiːkaɾika്kaːniʋa uɳa്ʈaːka്kuna്n̪u
n̪ala്la aːt͡ʃaːɾam manasa്sinṯe jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa mat̪abaോɖʱam
at̪a്t̪aɾam t̪a്ɾit̪ala ʋiʃa്ʋaːsam eːṯṯaʋum ujarn̪a്n̪a bʱaka്t̪ijilaːɳa്
laːbʱam pa്ɾat̪iːka്ʂika്kaːt̪e arpa്pika്kuna്n̪a ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪aːl suːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu
sat̪a്ʋanṯe t̪ikaɲa്ɲa srɨʂa്ʈijaːɳa് jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa ʋiʃa്ʋaːsam
abʱimaːnapa്ɾakaʈanat̪a്t̪il kaːɳika്kuna്n̪a mat̪am
n̪ala്la ʋinaോd̪am aːɾaːɖʱana pa്ɾaʃasa്t̪i
aŋa്ŋanejuɭa്ɭat̪a്  ɲaːn ɾaːɟasat̪a്t̪il peʈa്ʈaʋanaːɳa് aʋiʋeːkaʋum ʋa്jart̪a്t̪ʰaʋumaːɳa്
bud̪a്ɖʱiʃuːna്jamaːja it͡ʃa്t͡ʃʰaje pina്t̪uʈaɾuna്n̪a mat̪am
sa്ʋajam piːɖipa്pika്kuka ala്leŋa്kil upad̪a്ɾaʋika്kaːn aɖʱikaːɾat̪a്t̪il ʋaɾika
maṯṯaൊn̪a്n̪a്t̪amasa്sinṯe iɾuʈa്ʈum asukʰaʋum
sa്n̪eːɦapuːrʋa്ʋam n̪alkuna്n̪a sama്maːnam ena്n̪a് parajuma്paോɭ
ipa്paോɭ ɲaːn sana്t̪aോʂat̪a്t̪aോʈe n̪alkaɳam aʋan eʈuka്kuma്paോɭ
ona്n̪um t̪iɾike n̪alkaːnaːʋila്la jat̪ʰaːsa്t̪ʰaːnat̪a്t̪a് uɳa്ʈaːka്ki
n̪iʃa്t͡ʃit̪a samajaʋum oɾu miːṯṯa് sa്ʋiːkart̪a്t̪aːʋina്
sat̪a്ʋanṯe d̪aːnamaːɳa് n̪a്jaːjaʋum laːbʱakaɾaʋumaːɳa്
sa്ʋaːrt̪a്t̪ʰamaːji n̪alkija sama്maːnam eʋiʈe sa്ʋiːkaɾika്kaɳam
ʋiːɳa്ʈum pa്ɾat̪iːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u ala്leŋa്kil ena്t̪eŋa്kilum aʋasaːnam t̪eːʈuma്paോɭ
ala്leŋa്kil ʋid̪a്ʋeːʂat̪a്t̪aോʈe sama്maːnam n̪alkuna്n̪iʈat̪a്t̪a്
it̪a് ɾaːɟasinret̪aːɳa് pa്ɾeːɾaɳajaːl malinamaːja asukʰam
sama്maːnam maോʃamaːja samajat̪a്t̪a് erijapa്peʈa്ʈu
t̪eṯṯaːja sa്t̪ʰalat̪a്t̪a് aʈisa്t̪ʰaːna sa്ʋiːkart̪a്t̪aːʋina്
aʋaɦeːɭanat̪a്t̪ilaോ kaʈʰinamaːja d̪ajajila്laːja്majilaോ uɳa്ʈaːka്kijat̪a്
t̪amasa്sinṯe d̪aːnam iɾuɳa്ʈat̪aːɳa് at̪a് anuɡa്ɾaɦika്kila്la#
iʋiʈe ad̪a്ɖʱa്jaːjam  bʱaɡaʋad̪a് ɡiːt̪ajuʈe

krɨʂa്ɳan

eŋa്kilum aː una്n̪at̪amaːja pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ikaɭ paോlum paɾiʃiːlika്kaɳam
aṯṯaːt͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്menṯum ela്laː pʰalaŋa്ŋaɭum ʋiʈa്ʈukaൊʈuka്kuna്n̪at̪il
ʋarka്kukaɭ n̪irma്mit͡ʃa്t͡ʃat̪a് it̪aːɳa് enṯe ʋiɖʱi ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
it̪a് enṯe amuːla്jaʋum sa്t̪ʰiɾaʋumaːja ut̪a്t̪aɾaʋa്
n̪ird̪a്d̪eːʃit͡ʃa്t͡ʃiʈa്ʈuɭa്ɭa oɾu ɟaോlijil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋiʈa്ʈunilka്kal

iɾuʈa്ʈil n̪ina്n̪um ʋibʱa്ɾaːna്t̪ijil n̪ina്n̪um at̪a് paʈʰipa്pika്kuna്n̪u
maːmsat̪a്t̪ina് ɦaːnikaɾamaːja oɾu ɟaോlijil n̪ina്n̪a് ʋiʈa്ʈunilka്kal

at̪a്t̪aɾat̪a്t̪iluɭa്ɭa oɾaːɭ abʱiniʋeːʃat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u n̪eːʈa്ʈamila്la

opa്pam mad̪a്jaʋarɟa്ɟanaʋum aːɾaːɳa് aŋa്ŋane kaʈamakaɭ t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪at̪a്

mukʰasa്t̪ut̪ijila്laːt̪a്t̪a sa്ʋana്t̪am ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪il n̪a്jaːjiːkaɾika്kapa്peʈa്ʈa
samʋaːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭum samʃajaŋa്ŋaɭum upeːka്ʂika്kuka ad̪a്d̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inṯe sat̪a്ja pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ijaːɳa്
ena്t̪ena്n̪aːl ʃaɾiːɾat̪a്t̪il aːjiɾika്kuma്paോɭ aːrka്kum n̪ilka്kaːn kaɻijila്la
pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪a് puːrɳa്ɳamaːjum akana്n̪u ena്n̪iʈa്ʈum aːɾaːɳa് ʋiʈa്ʈunilka്kuna്n̪at̪a്

ariʋila്laːja്‌majaːl aːɾeŋa്kilum sa്ʋajam kaːɳuna്n̪u

kaɭaŋa്kamila്laːt̪a്t̪a manasa്sumaːji sa്ʋajam akana്n̪unilka്kuna്n̪u
kaൊla്laːn leːlam ʋiɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് apa്purat̪a്t̪uɭa്ɭa ela്laː aːt̪it̪ʰeːjaɾejum kaൊla്laɳam

ariʋa് arijaːʋuna്n̪a kaːɾa്jam arijuna്n̪a manasa്sa്

abʱinajam n̪aʈan upakaɾaɳam

muːna്n̪a് ʋibʱaɟika്kuna്n̪a ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭaːl ipa്paോɭ keːɭka്kuː
aʋaje ʋibʱaɟika്kuna്n̪a ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭ
jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰa ariʋuɳa്ʈa് it̪a് it̪aːɳa് ena്n̪a് manasilaːka്kuka
ela്laː ɟiːʋit̪aŋa്ŋaɭilum maːṯṯamila്laːt̪a്t̪a oɾu ɟiːʋit̪am kaːɳaːn
ʋeːrpiɾijalilum ʋeːrt̪iɾika്kaːnaːʋaːt̪a്t̪a ona്n̪a്
apuːrɳa്ɳamaːja ariʋuɳa്ʈa് kaːɳuna്n̪at̪a്
ʋeːriʈa്ʈa asa്t̪it̪a്ʋaŋa്ŋaɭ
kuːʈaːt̪e ʋeːrpiɾijuna്n̪at̪a് aʋaɾe jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰamaːji n̪ilanirt̪a്t̪una്n̪u
t̪eṯṯaːja ariʋuɳa്ʈa് ana്ɖʱamaːji paṯṯit͡ʃa്t͡ʃeːrn̪a്n̪at̪a്
oɾu kaːɾaɳaʋum ana്ʋeːʂika്kaːt̪e ela്laːʋaɾum ena്n̪a maʈa്ʈil oɾaːɭka്ka്
ʋeɭit͡ʃa്t͡ʃam n̪aʂa്ʈapa്peʈa്ʈat̪um iʈuŋa്ŋijat̪um maŋa്ŋijat̪um iɾuɳa്ʈat̪um
ʃaɾijaːja pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anamuɳa്ʈa് kalpa്pika്kapa്peʈa്ʈat̪a്
aṯṯaːt͡ʃa്t͡ʃa്‌menṯila്laːt̪e ʋikaːɾaɾaɦit̪amaːji
kaʈamaja്ka്ka് ʋeːɳa്ʈi sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪inaോ ʋid̪a്ʋeːʂat̪a്t̪inaോ n̪eːʈa്ʈat̪a്t̪inaോ ʋeːɳa്ʈijala്la
ʋa്jart̪a്t̪ʰamaːja pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anamuɳa്ʈa് manuʂa്jar pina്t̪uʈaɾuna്n̪at̪a്
aːɡa്ɾaɦaŋa്ŋaɭe t̪rɨpa്t̪ipa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːn ʋeːd̪anika്kuna്n̪u pa്ɾeːɾipa്pika്kuna്n̪u
sa്ʋajam baോɖʱat̪a്t̪aːl ela്laːm uɭka്kaൊɭa്ɭuna്n̪a sama്mard̪a്d̪at̪a്t̪aോʈe
it̪a് ɾaːɟasat̪a്t̪il n̪ina്n̪uɭa്ɭat̪aːɳa്  ʋikaːɾaːɖʱiːnaʋum ʋa്jart̪a്t̪ʰaʋumaːɳa്
iɾuɳa്ʈa pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anamuɳa്ʈa് oɾaːɭ oɾu kaːɾa്jam t͡ʃeja്juma്paോɭ
pa്ɾaʃa്n̪aŋa്ŋaɭeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് aʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱa upad̪a്ɾaʋat̪a്t̪eka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് aʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱa
ala്leŋa്kil maṯṯuɭa്ɭaʋarka്ka് t̪eṯṯa് aʋan upad̪a്ɾaʋit͡ʃa്t͡ʃaːl aʃa്ɾad̪a്ɖʱa
aʋanṯe sa്ʋana്t̪am aːt̪a്maːʋa്  karut̪a്t̪at̪um t͡ʃiːt̪a്t̪ajumaːja t̪amasa്sa്
ʃaɾijaːja t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪aʋan uɳa്ʈa് pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋan
sa്ʋajam ana്ʋeːʂika്kuna്n̪at̪il n̪ina്n̪a് muka്t̪an ʋinajam d̪rɨɖʱaniʃa്t͡ʃajam
urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃunilka്kuka n̪ala്lat̪aːjaːlum t̪ina്majaːjaːlum oɾupaോlejaːɳa്
ʃaɾijaːji t͡ʃeja്jaːnuɭa്ɭa uɭa്ɭaʈaka്kamaʋan ʃaɾika്kum pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪u
aːʋeːʃat̪a്t̪aോʈe t͡ʃeja്juna്n̪a oɾu ʋa്jaka്t̪ijuɳa്ʈa് pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪ika്kuna്n̪aʋan
pa്ɾeːɾaɳajil n̪ina്n̪a് laːbʱam t̪eːʈuna്n̪at̪a് paɾuʂaʋum ɖʱai̯ɾa്jaʋum
marikaʈaka്kaːn at͡ʃaɲa്t͡ʃalamaːja maːrimaːri aʈima
d̪uɦkʰat̪a്t̪inṯejum sana്t̪aോʂat̪a്t̪inṯejum ɾaɟasa് aʋan
d̪uʂa്pa്ɾaʋrɨt̪a്t̪ika്kaːr uɳa്ʈaːkum ajaɲa്ɲa ɦrɨd̪ajam
t̪aːɻa്n̪a്n̪a t͡ʃina്t̪aːɡat̪ika്kaːɾan ʃaːʈʰa്jam ʋaɲa്t͡ʃana ʋiʈa്ʈuʋiːɻa്t͡ʃa
muʂiɲa്ɲa mana്d̪aɡat̪ijiluɭa്ɭa n̪iɾaːʃajuɭa്ɭa  iɾuʈa്ʈinṯe kuʈa്ʈikaɭ
bud̪a്ɖʱijum d̪rɨɖʱat̪ajum kuːʈi keːɭka്kuː
muːna്n̪iɾaʈa്ʈi ʋeːrpiɾijal ɟeːt̪aːʋa്ɾaːɟakumaːɾan
ɡuɳaŋa്ŋaɭaːl iʋaje eŋa്ŋane ʋeːrt̪iɾika്kuna്n̪u
ɡa്ɾaɦika്kuna്n̪a bud̪a്ɖʱijaːɳa് n̪ala്lat̪a്
ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe ʋaɾaʋum t̪iɾit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu paോka്kum

ena്t̪ine bʱajapa്peʈaɳam ena്t̪ine bʱajapa്peʈaɾut̪a്
ena്t̪aːɳa് aːt̪a്maːʋine bana്ɖʱipa്pika്kuna്n̪at̪um maോt͡ʃipa്pika്kuna്n̪at̪um
at̪a് sat̪a്ʋanṯet̪aːɳa് ɾaːɟakumaːɾan sukʰam ena്n̪at̪inṯe
ʃaɾijaːji arijaːʋuna്n̪a bud̪a്ɖʱijaːɳa് maːɾaɖa്
t̪eṯṯa് ena്t̪aːɳa് n̪ala്lat̪a് ena്n̪arijuna്n̪u

urat͡ʃa്t͡ʃa manasa്saോʈejaോ ʃaːna്t̪amaːja sat̪a്jam paോlejaോ ala്la
it̪a് ɾaːɟaːsinṯet̪aːɳa് ɾaːɟakumaːɾan opa്pam abʱiniʋeːʃam
ana്ɖʱakaːɾat̪a്t̪il paൊt̪iɲa്ɲa bud̪a്ɖʱijaːɳa് t̪ina്ma
t̪eṯṯine ʃaɾijaːji kaːɳuna്n̪u ela്laːm kaːɳuna്n̪u
sat̪a്jat̪a്t̪inu ʋiɾud̪a്ɖʱamaːji ɦeː prɨt̪ʰajuʈe put̪a്ɾaː
at̪a് t̪amasa്sinṯet̪aːɳa് iɾuʈa്ʈum n̪iɾaːʃajum
oɾu manuʂa്janṯe sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪ajaːɳa് n̪ala്lat̪a്
aʋanṯe ɦrɨd̪ajamiʈipa്pukaɭ aʋanṯe ʃa്ʋaːsam t̪ana്n̪e
ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inṯe aʋanṯe ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe pa്ɾaʋart̪a്t̪anam n̪iʃa്t͡ʃit̪a
oɾika്kalum iɭakaːt̪a്t̪a ʋiʃa്ʋaːsat̪a്t̪ilum bʱaka്t̪ijilum
at̪a് sat̪a്ʋanṯet̪aːɳa് ɾaːɟakumaːɾan ʃaːna്t̪aʋum n̪a്jaːjaʋum
oɾu manuʂa്janṯe sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪ajaːɳa് kaɭaŋa്kam
aʋanṯe kaʈama laka്ʂa്jam paɾiʃa്ɾamam aʋasaːnam
ɟiːʋit̪at̪a്t̪inuʋeːɳa്ʈijum sama്pat̪a്t̪inaോʈuɭa്ɭa sa്n̪eːɦat̪a്t̪ina് ʋeːɳa്ʈijum
arɟa്ɟunaː ɾaːɟaːsa് paːʂan sa്ṯṯaːma്pa്ɖa്
ʋiɖa്ɖʱijuʈe sa്t̪ʰiɾat̪a d̪uɦkʰakaɾamaːɳa്
aʋanṯe alasat̪ajaോʈum saŋa്kaʈat̪a്t̪aോʈum bʱajat̪a്t̪aോʈum t͡ʃeːrn̪a്n̪unilka്kuna്n̪u
aʋanṯe maɳa്ʈat̪a്t̪aɾaʋum n̪iɾaːʃajum it̪a്prɨt̪ajuʈe makan

inijum keːɭka്kuː bʱaɾat̪anmaːɾuʈe aɖʱipan ena്n̪ila് n̪ina്n̪um
aʋiʈejuɭa്ɭa muːna്n̪a് t̪aɾat̪a്t̪iluɭa്ɭa aːnan̪a്d̪aŋa്ŋaɭ
n̪ala്la aːnan̪a്d̪am ena്n̪at̪a് n̪ilanilka്kuna്n̪a aːnan̪a്d̪amaːɳa്

ina്d̪a്ɾijaŋa്ŋaɭka്kum ina്d̪a്ɾijalaോkat̪a്t̪inum iʈajil maɖʱuɾam

ena്n̪ena്n̪eːka്kumaːji n̪irɟiːʋamaːja aːɡa്ɾaɦaŋa്ŋaɭ pʰalaŋa്ŋaɭ t̪a്jaɟit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu

ba്ɾaɦa്mam paɾamaോn̪a്n̪at̪an ela്laːʋaɾuʈejum eːṯṯaʋum ujarn̪a്n̪a ujaɾam
samarpa്pit̪an  ʃud̪a്ɖʱamaːja samjamanat̪a്t̪aോʈe ʋaɭarn̪a്n̪a ɦrɨd̪ajat̪a്t̪aോʈe
pa്ɾabʱut̪a്ʋamuɭa്ɭa aːt̪a്manijana്t̪a്ɾaɳat̪a്t̪il kut̪ana്t̪a്ɾaŋa്ŋaɭ upeːka്ʂika്kuna്n̪u

# t͡ʃila aːʋart̪a്t̪ana ʋaɾikaɭ iʋiʈe oɻiʋaːka്kijiɾika്kuna്n̪u

# ʋai̯d̪ika mat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe saːŋa്keːt̪ika ʋaːka്jaŋa്ŋaɭ

# iː bʱaːɡam muɻuʋanum ʋaɭaɾe uɭpa്peʈa്ʈiɾika്kuna്n̪at̪um renɖar t͡ʃeja്jaːn pa്ɾajaːsamuɭa്ɭat̪umaːɳa്

# saːmkʰa്jaːnan̪ejum jaോɡinan̪ejum iʋiʈe art̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪il maːṯṯaɳamena്n̪a് enika്ka് baോɖʱa്jamuɳa്ʈa്

# iʋiʈe krɨt̪a്jat̪ajeka്kurit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa് enika്ka് samʃajamuɳa്ʈa്

# suːɾa്janṯe oɾu peːɾa്

# pʰalam aːɡa്ɾaɦika്kaːt̪e

# at̪aːjat̪a് sana്t̪aോʂaʋum d̪uɦkʰaʋum ʋiɟajaʋum paɾaːɟajaʋum t͡ʃuːʈum t̪aɳupa്pum&

# at̪aːjat̪a് ʃaɾiːɾam

# samsa്‌krɨt̪at̪a്t̪il aːt̪a്maːʋinṯe iɾaʈa്ʈa art̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪il iː n̪aːʈakamuɳa്ʈa്

# aŋa്ŋane jat̪ʰaːrt̪a്t̪ʰat̪a്t̪il

# t̪aːɻa്n̪a്n̪at̪um pai̯ʃaːt͡ʃikaʋumaːja sa്ʋabʱaːʋamuɭa്ɭaʋar

# krɨʂa്ɳa

# ɲaːn iʋiʈe ɟana്mam ʋaːjit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu ɟanan̪am ɟaːɾa ala്la pa്ɾaːjam

# t͡ʃila ʋeːd̪aːna്t̪ikaɭuʈe samʃajaːt̪iːt̪amaːja oɾu inṯarpaോɭeːʂanaːji ɲaːn iʋiʈe pat̪a്t̪a് ʋaɾi samsa്‌krɨt̪a paːʈʰaŋa്ŋaɭ upeːka്ʂit͡ʃa്t͡ʃu

# miːṯṯarile maːṯṯam kaൊɳa്ʈa് ɲaːn aʈajaːɭapa്peʈut̪a്t̪aːn ʃa്ɾamit͡ʃa്t͡ʃa ʃai̯lijuʈejum ɾiːt̪ijuʈejum ujart͡ʃa്t͡ʃajileːka്ka് iʋiʈe samsa്‌krɨt̪a kaʋit̪a ujaɾuna്n̪u

# aɦinsa

# anaʃa്ʋaɾat̪ajuʈe amrɨt̪a്

# d̪a ɟaːpa്pa് ena്n̪a് ʋiɭika്kuna്n̪u

# samsa്krɨt̪a pad̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe samjuka്t̪a ɾuːpam

# kamalaːpat̪a്ɾaːka്ʂa

# iʋajela്laːm ɦina്d̪upana്t̪ijaോɳinṯe d̪ai̯ʋikamaോ d̪ai̯ʋikamaോ aːja ut̪a്t̪aɾaʋukaɭaːɳa്

# d̪ai̯ʋaŋa്ŋaɭuʈe d̪ai̯ʋameː n̪inaka്ku ʋana്d̪anam anukuːlamaːjiɾika്kuː

# kaːṯṯa്

# n̪aോʈa്ʈa് n̪aോka്kuna്n̪ila്lanapeːka്ʂa

# maɦaːbʱaːɾat̪at̪a്t̪inṯe kalka്kaʈa്ʈa pat̪ipa്pil iː muːna്n̪a് oːpa്paɳimɡa് lai̯nukaɭ uɳa്ʈa്

# it̪a് ka്ʂeːt̪a്ɾaka്ʂeːt̪a്ɾaɟa്ɲaːnajaോɟa്‌n̪aːnan jat̪a് t̪aɟa്‌n̪aːn mat̪an mamajuʈe saːɖʱa്jamaːja eːṯṯaʋum aʈut̪a്t̪uɭa്ɭa pat̪ipa്paːɳa്

# samsa്‌krɨt̪at̪a്t̪inṯe ɾaɳa്ʈa് ʋaɾikaɭ ɲaːn iʋiʈe oɻiʋaːka്kuna്n̪u pa്ɾat̪a്jaka്ʂat̪a്t̪il t͡ʃila ʋeːd̪aːna്t̪ikaɭ inṯarpaോɭeːṯṯa് t͡ʃeja്t̪u

# ɡarbʱapaːt̪a്ɾaŋa്ŋaɭ

# ɲaːn iʋiʈe samsa്‌krɨt̪a ʃa്laോkaŋa്ŋaɭ paɾiɡaɳika്kuna്n̪ila്laʋeːd̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe aɖʱikaːɾat̪a്t̪inet̪iɾaːja aːka്ɾamaɳam misa്ṯṯar ɖeːʋisinaൊpa്pam ena്n̪aːl manaോɦaɾamaːja oɾu ɡaːnaɾat͡ʃana oɾu put̪ija at̪a്t̪ijuʈe upama ʋrɨka്ʂam

# ɲaːn iʋiʈe oɾu ʋaːka്jam oɻiʋaːka്kuna്n̪u pa്ɾat̪a്jaka്ʂat̪a്t̪il inṯarpaോɭeːṯṯaɖa്

# asuɾana്maːɾuʈe liṯṯa്

# misa്ṯṯar ɖeːʋisinaൊpa്pam aʋasaːnika്kuna്n̪a pat̪a്t̪a് ʃa്laോkaŋa്ŋaɭ ɲaːn oɻiʋaːka്kuna്n̪u

# ɾaːka്ʂasana്maːɾum jaka്ʂana്maːɾum muːrt̪a്t̪iːbʱaːʋamila്laːt̪a്t̪aʋaɾum ena്n̪aːl maɦat̪a്t̪aːja ʃaka്t̪ijum sama്maːnaŋa്ŋaɭum sau̯na്d̪aɾa്jaʋumuɭa്ɭa at̪eː samajam sau̯ma്jat̪ajuɭa്ɭaʋaɾaːɳa്

# iʋa d̪uʂa്ʈa alaɲa്ɲut̪iɾijuna്n̪a pa്ɾeːt̪aŋa്ŋaɭuʈe aːt̪a്maːka്kaɭaːɳa്

# jat̪ajamaːn ɾaːt̪a്ɾijuʈe kaːʋalinuʃeːʂam aʋaʃeːʂika്kuna്n̪a bʱaka്ʂaɳam ina്t̪a്jajil it̪a് oɾupaka്ʂeː maോʃamaːkum

# ʋaɭaɾe samʃajaːsa്pad̪amaːja aːɖʱikaːɾikat̪ajaːl ɲaːn samaːpana ʃa്laോkaŋa്ŋaɭ oɻiʋaːka്kuna്n̪u











aɟa്ɲaːt̪an eɻut̪ija bʱaɡaʋad̪a് ɡiːt̪ajuʈe pa്ɾaോɟaka്ṯṯa് ɡuʈa്ʈanbarɡa് ibuka്kinṯe aʋasaːnam

*** iː pad̪a്ɖʱat̪ijuʈe aʋasaːnam ɡuʈa്ʈanberɡa് ibuka്ka് bʱaɡaʋad̪a്ɡiːt̪a ***

***** iː fajalina്  ala്leŋa്kil  ena്n̪a് peːɾiʈaɳam *****
it̪um ʋiʋiɖʱa faോrmaːṯṯukaɭuʈe ela്laː anubana്ɖʱa fajalukaɭum it̪il kaːɳaːm
